## Goroutines
_Tools for managing and working with Goroutines._

- [anchor](https://github.com/kyuff/anchor) ⭐ 4 - Updated Apr 2026: Library to manage component lifecycle in microservice architectures.
- [ants](https://github.com/panjf2000/ants) ⭐ 14466 - Updated Jul 2026: A high-performance and low-cost goroutine pool in Go.
- [artifex](https://github.com/borderstech/artifex) ⭐ 214 - Updated Jul 2024: Simple in-memory job queue for Golang using worker-based dispatching.
- [async](https://github.com/yaitoo/async) ⭐ 16 - Updated Mar 2024: An asynchronous task package with async/await style for Go.
- [async](https://github.com/reugn/async) ⭐ 309 - Updated Jan 2026: An alternative sync library for Go (Future, Promise, Locks).
- [async](https://github.com/studiosol/async) ⭐ 140 - Updated Nov 2020: A safe way to execute functions asynchronously, recovering them in case of panic.
- [async-job](https://github.com/lab210-dev/async-job) ⭐ 12 - Updated May 2022: AsyncJob is an asynchronous queue job manager with light code, clear and speed.
- [breaker](https://github.com/kamilsk/breaker) ⭐ 21 - Updated May 2021: Flexible mechanism to make execution flow interruptible.
- [channelify](https://github.com/ddelizia/channelify) ⭐ 34 - Updated Oct 2020: Transform your function to return channels for easy and powerful parallel processing.
- [conc](https://github.com/sourcegraph/conc) ⭐ 10417 - Updated Jan 2024: conc is your toolbelt for structured concurrency in go, making common tasks easier and safer.
- [concurrency-limiter](https://github.com/vivek-ng/concurrency-limiter) ⭐ 19 - Updated Mar 2026: Concurrency limiter with support for timeouts, dynamic priority and context cancellation of goroutines.
- [conexec](https://github.com/ITcathyh/conexec) ⭐ 18 - Updated May 2026: A concurrent toolkit to help execute funcs concurrently in an efficient and safe way. It supports specifying the overall timeout to avoid blocking and uses goroutine pool to improve efficiency.
- [cyclicbarrier](https://github.com/marusama/cyclicbarrier) ⭐ 158 - Updated Jun 2020: CyclicBarrier for golang.
- [execpool](https://github.com/hexdigest/execpool) ⭐ 29 - Updated Jul 2021: A pool built around exec.Cmd that spins up a given number of processes in advance and attaches stdin and stdout to them when needed. Very similar to FastCGI or Apache Prefork MPM but works for any command.
- [flowmatic](https://github.com/carlmjohnson/flowmatic) ⭐ 402 - Updated Jun 2024: Structured concurrency made easy.
- [go-accumulator](https://github.com/nar10z/go-accumulator) ⭐ 11 - Updated Jun 2026: Solution for accumulation of events and their subsequent processing.
- [go-actor](https://github.com/vladopajic/go-actor) ⭐ 302 - Updated Jul 2026: A tiny library for writing concurrent programs using actor model.
- [go-floc](https://github.com/workanator/go-floc) ⭐ 269 - Updated Aug 2021: Orchestrate goroutines with ease.
- [go-flow](https://github.com/kamildrazkiewicz/go-flow) ⭐ 221 - Updated Sep 2017: Control goroutines execution order.
- [go-tools/multithreading](https://github.com/nikhilsaraf/go-tools) ⭐ 17 - Updated Mar 2019: Manage a pool of goroutines using this lightweight library with a simple API.
- [go-trylock](https://github.com/subchen/go-trylock) ⭐ 36 - Updated May 2021: TryLock support on read-write lock for Golang.
- [go-waitgroup](https://github.com/pieterclaerhout/go-waitgroup) ⭐ 49 - Updated Sep 2025: Like sync.WaitGroup with error handling and concurrency control.
- [go-workerpool](https://github.com/zenthangplus/go-workerpool) ⭐ 13 - Updated Aug 2022: Inspired from Java Thread Pool, Go WorkerPool aims to control heavy Go Routines.
- [goccm](https://github.com/zenthangplus/goccm) ⭐ 73 - Updated Jan 2023: Go Concurrency Manager package limits the number of goroutines that allowed to run concurrently.
- [gohive](https://github.com/loveleshsharma/gohive) ⭐ 54 - Updated Nov 2023: A highly performant and easy to use Goroutine pool for Go.
- [gollback](https://github.com/vardius/gollback) ⭐ 123 - Updated Feb 2023: asynchronous simple function utilities, for managing execution of closures and callbacks.
- [gowl](https://github.com/hamed-yousefi/gowl) ⭐ 71 - Updated Oct 2023: Gowl is a process management and process monitoring tool at once. An infinite worker pool gives you the ability to control the pool and processes and monitor their status.
- [goworker](https://github.com/benmanns/goworker) ⭐ 2847 - Updated Apr 2025: goworker is a Go-based background worker.
- [gowp](https://github.com/xxjwxc/gowp) ⭐ 516 - Updated Sep 2024: gowp is concurrency limiting goroutine pool.
- [gpool](https://github.com/Sherifabdlnaby/gpool) ⭐ 90 - Updated Jul 2026: manages a resizeable pool of context-aware goroutines to bound concurrency.
- [grpool](https://github.com/ivpusic/grpool) ⭐ 735 - Updated Aug 2017: Lightweight Goroutine pool.
- [hands](https://github.com/duanckham/hands) ⭐ 10 - Updated Aug 2025: A process controller used to control the execution and return strategies of multiple goroutines.
- [Hunch](https://github.com/AaronJan/Hunch) ⭐ 104 - Updated May 2022 - ⚠️ Archived: Hunch provides functions like: All, First, Retry, Waterfall etc., that makes asynchronous flow control more intuitive.
- [kyoo](https://github.com/dirkaholic/kyoo) ⭐ 51 - Updated Mar 2026: Provides an unlimited job queue and concurrent worker pools.
- [neilotoole/errgroup](https://github.com/neilotoole/errgroup) ⭐ 163 - Updated Jan 2023: Drop-in alternative to sync/errgroup, limited to a pool of N worker goroutines.
- [nursery](https://github.com/arunsworld/nursery) ⭐ 71 - Updated Jul 2021: Structured concurrency in Go.
- [oversight](https://pkg.go.dev/cirello.io/oversight): Oversight is a complete implementation of the Erlang supervision trees.
- [parallel-fn](https://github.com/rafaeljesus/parallel-fn) ⭐ 37 - Updated Jan 2018: Run functions in parallel.
- [pond](https://github.com/alitto/pond) ⭐ 2172 - Updated Apr 2026: Minimalistic and High-performance goroutine worker pool written in Go.
- [pool](https://github.com/go-playground/pool) ⭐ 724 - Updated Aug 2016: Limited consumer goroutine or unlimited goroutine pool for easier goroutine handling and cancellation.
- [rill](https://github.com/destel/rill) ⭐ 1847 - Updated Jul 2026: Go toolkit for clean, composable, channel-based concurrency.
- [routine](https://github.com/timandy/routine) ⭐ 292 - Updated May 2026: routine is a ThreadLocal for go library. It encapsulates and provides some easy-to-use, non-competitive, high-performance goroutine context access interfaces, which can help you access coroutine context information more gracefully.
- [routine](https://github.com/x-mod/routine) ⭐ 63 - Updated May 2026: go routine control with context, support: Main, Go, Pool and some useful Executors.
- [semaphore](https://github.com/kamilsk/semaphore) ⭐ 102 - Updated Apr 2020: Semaphore pattern implementation with timeout of lock/unlock operations based on channel and context.
- [semaphore](https://github.com/marusama/semaphore) ⭐ 178 - Updated Mar 2021: Fast resizable semaphore implementation based on CAS (faster than channel-based semaphore implementations).
- [stl](https://github.com/ssgreg/stl) ⭐ 31 - Updated Oct 2019: Software transactional locks based on Software Transactional Memory (STM) concurrency control mechanism.
- [threadpool](https://github.com/shettyh/threadpool) ⭐ 103 - Updated Mar 2020: Golang threadpool implementation.
- [tunny](https://github.com/Jeffail/tunny) ⭐ 4033 - Updated Jul 2021: Goroutine pool for golang.
- [worker-pool](https://github.com/vardius/worker-pool) ⭐ 93 - Updated Jan 2021: goworker is a Go simple async worker pool.
- [workerpool](https://github.com/gammazero/workerpool) ⭐ 1460 - Updated Jul 2026: Goroutine pool that limits the concurrency of task execution, not the number of tasks queued.
- [autopool](https://github.com/AshvinBambhaniya/autopool) ⭐ 5 - Updated Jul 2026: Zero-config, auto-scaling worker pool for Go with priority-aware scheduling.

## Hardware

- [arduino-cli](https://github.com/arduino/arduino-cli) ⭐ 4966 - Updated Jul 2026: Official Arduino CLI and library. Can run standalone, or be incorporated into larger Go projects.

## Job Scheduler
_Libraries for scheduling jobs._

- [cdule](https://github.com/deepaksinghvi/cdule) ⭐ 61 - Updated Aug 2025: Job scheduler library with database support
- [cheek](https://github.com/bart6114/cheek) ⭐ 199 - Updated Mar 2026: A simple crontab like scheduler that aims to offer a KISS approach to job scheduling.
- [clockwerk](https://github.com/onatm/clockwerk) ⭐ 183 - Updated Nov 2024: Go package to schedule periodic jobs using a simple, fluent syntax.
- [cronticker](https://github.com/krayzpipes/cronticker) ⭐ 20 - Updated Jan 2021: A ticker implementation to support cron schedules.
- [go-cron](https://github.com/rk/go-cron) ⭐ 239 - Updated Feb 2020: Simple Cron library for go that can execute closures or functions at varying intervals, from once a second to once a year on a specific date and time. Primarily for web applications and long running daemons.
- [go-cron](https://github.com/netresearch/go-cron) ⭐ 49 - Updated Jun 2026: Cron job scheduler with runtime schedule updates, per-entry context, resilience middleware (retry, circuit breaker, rate limiting), and observability hooks; successor to robfig/cron.
- [go-job](https://github.com/cybergarage/go-job) ⭐ 2 - Updated Mar 2026: A flexible and extensible job scheduling and execution library for Go.
- [go-quartz](https://github.com/reugn/go-quartz) ⭐ 2014 - Updated Jan 2026: Simple, zero-dependency scheduling library for Go.
- [go-scheduler](https://github.com/pardnchiu/go-scheduler) ⭐ 36 - Updated Jul 2026: Job scheduler supporting standard cron expressions, custom descriptors, intervals, and task dependencies.
- [gocron](https://github.com/go-co-op/gocron) ⭐ 7105 - Updated Jul 2026: Easy and fluent Go job scheduling. This is an actively maintained fork of jasonlvhit/gocron.
- [goflow](https://github.com/fieldryand/goflow) ⭐ 481 - Updated Jul 2024: A simple but powerful DAG scheduler and dashboard.
- [gron](https://github.com/roylee0704/gron) ⭐ 1034 - Updated Jun 2016: Define time-based tasks using a simple Go API and Gron’s scheduler will run them accordingly.
- [gronx](https://github.com/adhocore/gronx) ⭐ 512 - Updated May 2026: Cron expression parser, task runner and daemon consuming crontab like task list.
- [JobRunner](https://github.com/bamzi/jobrunner) ⭐ 1090 - Updated Oct 2019: Smart and featureful cron job scheduler with job queuing and live monitoring built in.
- [leprechaun](https://github.com/kilgaloon/leprechaun) ⭐ 106 - Updated Jul 2022: Job scheduler that supports webhooks, crons and classic scheduling.
- [ofelia](https://github.com/netresearch/ofelia) ⭐ 63 - Updated Jul 2026: Docker job scheduler (crontab for Docker); fork of mcuadros/ofelia that adds a web UI, job dependencies, retries, and job persistence.
- [pending](https://github.com/kahoon/pending) ⭐ 7 - Updated Apr 2026: ID-based debounced task scheduler for deferred tasks with cancellation, graceful shutdown, and optional concurrency limits.
- [sched](https://github.com/romshark/sched) ⭐ 31 - Updated Feb 2025: A job scheduler with the ability to fast-forward time.
- [scheduler](https://github.com/carlescere/scheduler) ⭐ 469 - Updated Jan 2017: Cronjobs scheduling made easy.
- [scheduler](https://github.com/yuseferi/scheduler) ⭐ 6 - Updated Apr 2026: Go-native distributed job scheduler with delayed tasks, batched Redis coordination, retries, lease-based recovery, and versioned queue partitioning.
- [tasks](https://github.com/madflojo/tasks) ⭐ 331 - Updated Jun 2026: An easy to use in-process scheduler for recurring tasks in Go.
- [tickstem/cron](https://github.com/tickstem/cron) ⭐ 1 - Updated Apr 2026: Go client for scheduling HTTP cron jobs, with execution history, failure alerts, and tsk-local for testing handlers without live credentials.
- [tickstem/heartbeat](https://github.com/tickstem/heartbeat) ⭐ 1 - Updated May 2026: Go client for dead-man's switch heartbeat monitoring: ping a URL after each job run and get alerted by email if pings stop arriving.

## JSON

- [dynjson](https://github.com/cocoonspace/dynjson) ⭐ 16 - Updated Oct 2021: Client-customizable JSON formats for dynamic APIs.
- [ej](https://github.com/lucassscaravelli/ej) ⭐ 10 - Updated Apr 2020: Write and read JSON from different sources succinctly.
- [epoch](https://github.com/vtopc/epoch) ⭐ 17 - Updated Feb 2024: Contains primitives for marshaling/unmarshalling Unix timestamp/epoch to/from build-in time.Time type in JSON.
- [fastjson](https://github.com/valyala/fastjson) ⭐ 2462 - Updated Feb 2026: Fast JSON parser and validator for Go. No custom structs, no code generation, no reflection.
- [gabs](https://github.com/Jeffail/gabs) ⭐ 3531 - Updated Feb 2023: For parsing, creating and editing unknown or dynamic JSON in Go.
- [gjo](https://github.com/skanehira/gjo) ⭐ 132 - Updated Apr 2020: Small utility to create JSON objects.
- [GJSON](https://github.com/tidwall/gjson) ⭐ 15546 - Updated May 2026: Get a JSON value with one line of code.
- [go-jsonerror](https://github.com/ddymko/go-jsonerror) ⭐ 16 - Updated Oct 2019: Go-JsonError is meant to allow us to easily create json response errors that follow the JsonApi spec.

- [gojmapr](https://github.com/limiu82214/gojmapr) ⭐ 22 - Updated Jun 2023: Get simple struct from complex json by json path.
- [gojq](https://github.com/elgs/gojq) ⭐ 191 - Updated Jun 2023: JSON query in Golang.
- [gojson](https://github.com/ChimeraCoder/gojson) ⭐ 2688 - Updated Aug 2018: Automatically generate Go (golang) struct definitions from example JSON.
- [htmljson](https://github.com/nikolaydubina/htmljson) ⭐ 10 - Updated Jun 2026: Rich rendering of JSON as HTML in Go.
- [JayDiff](https://github.com/yazgazan/jaydiff) ⭐ 111 - Updated Apr 2026: JSON diff utility written in Go.
- [jettison](https://github.com/wI2L/jettison) ⭐ 180 - Updated Jan 2023: Fast and flexible JSON encoder for Go.
- [jscan](https://github.com/romshark/jscan) ⭐ 101 - Updated Jan 2024: High performance zero-allocation JSON iterator.
- [JSON-to-Go](https://mholt.github.io/json-to-go/): Convert JSON to Go struct.
- [JSON-to-Proto](https://json-to-proto.github.io/): Convert JSON to Protobuf online.
- [json2go](https://github.com/m-zajac/json2go) ⭐ 142 - Updated Mar 2026: Advanced JSON to Go struct conversion. Provides package that can parse multiple JSON documents and create struct to fit them all.
- [jsonapi-errors](https://github.com/AmuzaTkts/jsonapi-errors) ⭐ 13 - Updated Nov 2016: Go bindings based on the JSON API errors reference.
- [jsoncolor](https://github.com/neilotoole/jsoncolor) ⭐ 54 - Updated May 2026: Drop-in replacement for encoding/json that outputs colorized JSON.
- [jsondiff](https://github.com/wI2L/jsondiff) ⭐ 629 - Updated Apr 2026: JSON diff library for Go based on RFC6902 (JSON Patch).
- [jsonf](https://github.com/miolini/jsonf) ⭐ 64 - Updated Dec 2020: Console tool for highlighted formatting and struct query fetching JSON.
- [jsongo](https://github.com/ricardolonga/jsongo) ⭐ 108 - Updated Dec 2016: Fluent API to make it easier to create Json objects.
- [jsonhal](https://github.com/RichardKnop/jsonhal) ⭐ 13 - Updated Nov 2018: Simple Go package to make custom structs marshal into HAL compatible JSON responses.
- [jsonhandlers](https://github.com/abusomani/jsonhandlers) ⭐ 2 - Updated Mar 2023: JSON library to expose simple handlers that lets you easily read and write json from various sources.
- [jsonic](https://github.com/sinhashubham95/jsonic) ⭐ 11 - Updated Jan 2021: Utilities to handle and query JSON without defining structs in a type safe manner.
- [jsonvalue](https://github.com/Andrew-M-C/go.jsonvalue) ⭐ 203 - Updated Feb 2026: A fast and convenient library for unstructured JSON data, replacing encoding/json.
- [jzon](https://github.com/zerosnake0/jzon) ⭐ 11 - Updated Aug 2022: JSON library with standard compatible API/behavior.
- [kazaam](https://github.com/Qntfy/kazaam) ⭐ 293 - Updated Jul 2021: API for arbitrary transformation of JSON documents.
- [mapslice-json](https://github.com/mickep76/mapslice-json) ⭐ 20 - Updated Jul 2021: Go MapSlice for ordered marshal/ unmarshal of maps in JSON.
- [marshmallow](https://github.com/PerimeterX/marshmallow) ⭐ 391 - Updated Jul 2023: Performant JSON unmarshalling for flexible use cases.
- [mp](https://github.com/sanbornm/mp) ⭐ 47 - Updated May 2016: Simple cli email parser. It currently takes stdin and outputs JSON.
- [OjG](https://github.com/ohler55/ojg) ⭐ 952 - Updated Jul 2026: Optimized JSON for Go is a high performance parser with a variety of additional JSON tools including JSONPath.
- [omg.jsonparser](https://github.com/dedalqq/omg.jsonparser) ⭐ 6 - Updated Oct 2021: Simple JSON parser with validation by condition via golang struct fields tags.
- [SJSON](https://github.com/tidwall/sjson) ⭐ 2717 - Updated May 2026: Set a JSON value with one line of code.
- [ujson](https://github.com/olvrng/ujson) ⭐ 85 - Updated Jan 2025: Fast and minimal JSON parser and transformer that works on unstructured JSON.
- [vjson](https://github.com/miladibra10/vjson) ⭐ 41 - Updated Jul 2025: Go package for validating JSON objects with declaring a JSON schema with fluent API.

## Logging

- [go-cronowriter](https://github.com/utahta/go-cronowriter) ⭐ 56 - Updated Nov 2020: Simple writer that rotate log files automatically based on current date and time, like cronolog.
- [go-log](https://github.com/pieterclaerhout/go-log) ⭐ 11 - Updated Apr 2026: A logging library with stack traces, object dumping and optional timestamps.

- [go-logger](https://github.com/apsdehal/go-logger) ⭐ 288 - Updated May 2019: Simple logger of Go Programs, with level handlers.

- [gone/log](https://github.com/One-com/gone/tree/master/log): Fast, extendable, full-featured, std-lib source compatible log library.
- [httpretty](https://github.com/henvic/httpretty) ⭐ 414 - Updated Sep 2024: Pretty-prints your regular HTTP requests on your terminal for debugging (similar to http.DumpRequest).
- [journald](https://github.com/ssgreg/journald) ⭐ 46 - Updated Mar 2021: Go implementation of systemd Journal's native API for logging.
- [kemba](https://github.com/clok/kemba) ⭐ 18 - Updated Jan 2024: A tiny debug logging tool inspired by debug, great for CLI tools and applications.
- [lazyjournal](https://github.com/Lifailon/lazyjournal) ⭐ 1321 - Updated May 2026: A TUI for reading and filtering logs from journalctl, file system, Docker and Podman containers, as well Kubernetes pods.
- [log](https://github.com/aerogo/log) ⭐ 10 - Updated Oct 2019: An O(1) logging system that allows you to connect one log to multiple writers (e.g. stdout, a file and a TCP connection).
- [log](https://github.com/apex/log) ⭐ 1376 - Updated Aug 2020: Structured logging package for Go.
- [log](https://github.com/go-playground/log) ⭐ 293 - Updated Aug 2023: Simple, configurable and scalable Structured Logging for Go.
- [log](https://github.com/teris-io/log) ⭐ 25 - Updated Dec 2017: Structured log interface for Go cleanly separates logging facade from its implementation.
- [log](https://github.com/heartwilltell/log) ⭐ 17 - Updated Dec 2022: Simple leveled logging wrapper around standard log package.
- [log](https://github.com/no-src/log) ⭐ 4 - Updated Nov 2025: A simple logging framework out of the box.
- [log15](https://github.com/inconshreveable/log15) ⭐ 1104 - Updated May 2026: Simple, powerful logging for Go.
- [logdump](https://github.com/ewwwwwqm/logdump) ⭐ 11 - Updated Apr 2018: Package for multi-level logging.
- [logex](https://github.com/chzyer/logex) ⭐ 42 - Updated Apr 2024: Golang log lib, supports tracking and level, wrap by standard log lib.
- [logger](https://github.com/azer/logger) ⭐ 159 - Updated Jan 2026: Minimalistic logging library for Go.
- [logo](https://github.com/mbndr/logo) ⭐ 12 - Updated Dec 2020: Golang logger to different configurable writers.
- [logrus](https://github.com/Sirupsen/logrus) ⭐ 25750 - Updated Jun 2026: Structured logger for Go.
- [logrusiowriter](https://github.com/cabify/logrusiowriter) ⭐ 15 - Updated Oct 2024: io.Writer implementation using logrus logger.
- [logrusly](https://github.com/sebest/logrusly) ⭐ 29 - Updated Mar 2018: logrus plug-in to send errors to a Loggly.
- [logutils](https://github.com/hashicorp/logutils) ⭐ 372 - Updated Jan 2026: Utilities for slightly better logging in Go (Golang) extending the standard logger.
- [logxi](https://github.com/mgutz/logxi) ⭐ 356 - Updated Oct 2016: 12-factor app logger that is fast and makes you happy.
- [lumberjack](https://github.com/natefinch/lumberjack) ⭐ 5454 - Updated Feb 2023: Simple rolling logger, implements io.WriteCloser.
- [mlog](https://github.com/jbrodriguez/mlog) ⭐ 33 - Updated Aug 2018: Simple logging module for go, with 5 levels, an optional rotating logfile feature and stdout/stderr output.
- [noodlog](https://github.com/gyozatech/noodlog) ⭐ 44 - Updated Apr 2023: Parametrized JSON logging library which lets you obfuscate sensitive data and marshal any kind of content. No more printed pointers instead of values, nor escape chars for the JSON strings.
- [onelog](https://github.com/francoispqt/onelog) ⭐ 414 - Updated Mar 2019: Onelog is a dead simple but very efficient JSON logger. It is the fastest JSON logger out there in all scenarios. Also, it is one of the logger with the lowest allocation.
- [ozzo-log](https://github.com/go-ozzo/ozzo-log) ⭐ 123 - Updated Jul 2016: High performance logging supporting log severity, categorization, and filtering. Can send filtered log messages to various targets (e.g. console, network, mail).
- [phuslu/log](https://github.com/phuslu/log) ⭐ 870 - Updated Jul 2026: High performance structured logging.
- [pp](https://github.com/k0kubun/pp) ⭐ 2049 - Updated Jul 2026: Colored pretty printer for Go language.
- [rollingwriter](https://github.com/arthurkiller/rollingWriter) ⭐ 292 - Updated Oct 2023: RollingWriter is an auto-rotate io.Writer implementation with multi policies to provide log file rotation.
- [seelog](https://github.com/cihub/seelog) ⭐ 1636 - Updated Jan 2017: Logging functionality with flexible dispatching, filtering, and formatting.
- [sentry-go](https://github.com/getsentry/sentry-go) ⭐ 1098 - Updated Jul 2026: Sentry SDK for Go. Helps monitor and track errors with real-time alerts and performance monitoring.
- [slf4g](https://github.com/echocat/slf4g) ⭐ 6 - Updated Mar 2026: Simple Logging Facade for Golang: Simple structured logging; but powerful, extendable and customizable, with huge amount of learnings from decades of past logging frameworks.
- [slog](https://github.com/gookit/slog) ⭐ 548 - Updated Jul 2026: Lightweight, configurable, extensible logger for Go.
- [slog-formatter](https://github.com/samber/slog-formatter) ⭐ 220 - Updated Jul 2026: Common formatters for slog and helpers to build your own.
- [slog-multi](https://github.com/samber/slog-multi) ⭐ 629 - Updated Jul 2026: Chain of slog.Handler (pipeline, fanout...).
- [slogor](https://gitlab.com/greyxor/slogor) ⭐ 18 - Updated Jul 2026: A colorful slog handler.
- [spew](https://github.com/davecgh/go-spew) ⭐ 6399 - Updated Aug 2018: Implements a deep pretty printer for Go data structures to aid in debugging.
- [sqldb-logger](https://github.com/simukti/sqldb-logger) ⭐ 382 - Updated Jan 2023: A logger for Go SQL database driver without modify existing \*sql.DB stdlib usage.
- [stdlog](https://github.com/alexcesaro/log) ⭐ 48 - Updated Sep 2015: Stdlog is an object-oriented library providing leveled logging. It is very useful for cron jobs.
- [structy/log](https://github.com/structy/log) ⭐ 5 - Updated Jan 2022: A simple to use log system, minimalist but with features for debugging and differentiation of messages.
- [tail](https://github.com/hpcloud/tail) ⭐ 2782 - Updated May 2018: Go package striving to emulate the features of the BSD tail program.
- [timberjack](https://github.com/DeRuina/timberjack) ⭐ 151 - Updated Jun 2026: Rolling logger with size-based, time-based, and scheduled clock-based rotation, supporting compression and cleanup.
- [tint](https://github.com/lmittmann/tint) ⭐ 1320 - Updated Jul 2026: A slog.Handler that writes tinted logs.
- [xlog](https://github.com/xfxdev/xlog) ⭐ 8 - Updated Jan 2019: Plugin architecture and flexible log system for Go, with level ctrl, multiple log target and custom log format.
- [xlog](https://github.com/rs/xlog) ⭐ 141 - Updated Dec 2017: Structured logger for net/context aware HTTP handlers with flexible dispatching.
- [xylog](https://github.com/xybor-x/xylog) ⭐ 17 - Updated Jan 2023: Leveled and structured logging, dynamic fields, high performance, zone management, simple configuration, and readable syntax.
- [yell](https://github.com/jfcg/yell) ⭐ 1 - Updated Mar 2022: Yet another minimalistic logging library.
- [zap](https://github.com/uber-go/zap) ⭐ 24577 - Updated Apr 2026: Fast, structured, leveled logging in Go.
- [zax](https://github.com/yuseferi/zax) ⭐ 37 - Updated Apr 2026: Integrate Context with Zap logger, which leads to more flexibility in Go logging.
- [zerolog](https://github.com/rs/zerolog) ⭐ 12474 - Updated Apr 2026: Zero-allocation JSON logger.
- [zkits-logger](https://github.com/edoger/zkits-logger) ⭐ 28 - Updated May 2023: A powerful zero-dependency JSON logger.
- [zl](https://github.com/nkmr-jp/zl) ⭐ 10 - Updated Apr 2026: High Developer Experience, zap based logger. It offers rich functionality but is easy to configure.

## Messaging
_Libraries that implement messaging systems._

- [ami](https://github.com/kak-tus/ami) ⭐ 34 - Updated Apr 2020: Go client to reliable queues based on Redis Cluster Streams.
- [amqp](https://github.com/rabbitmq/amqp091-go) ⭐ 2022 - Updated Jul 2026: Go RabbitMQ Client Library.
- [APNs2](https://github.com/sideshow/apns2) ⭐ 3184 - Updated Jul 2025: HTTP/2 Apple Push Notification provider for Go - Send push notifications to iOS, tvOS, Safari and OSX apps.
- [Asynq](https://github.com/hibiken/asynq) ⭐ 13527 - Updated Jun 2026: A simple, reliable, and efficient distributed task queue for Go built on top of Redis.
- [backlite](https://github.com/mikestefanello/backlite) ⭐ 150 - Updated Jul 2025: Type-safe, persistent, embedded task queues and background job runner w/ SQLite.
- [Beaver](https://github.com/Clivern/Beaver) ⭐ 1581 - Updated Dec 2023: A real time messaging server to build a scalable in-app notifications, multiplayer games, chat apps in web and mobile apps.
- [broker](https://github.com/qvcloud/broker) ⭐ 11 - Updated Jan 2026: Production-grade messaging abstraction with a unified API for various brokers and built-in OpenTelemetry integration.
- [Bus](https://github.com/mustafaturan/bus) ⭐ 369 - Updated May 2023: Minimalist message bus implementation for internal communication.
- [Centrifugo](https://github.com/centrifugal/centrifugo) ⭐ 10527 - Updated Jul 2026: Real-time messaging (Websockets or SockJS) server in Go.
- [Chanify](https://github.com/chanify/chanify) ⭐ 1322 - Updated Feb 2023: A push notification server send message to your iOS devices.
- [Commander](https://github.com/jeroenrinzema/commander) ⭐ 68 - Updated Apr 2021: A high-level event driven consumer/producer supporting various "dialects" such as Apache Kafka.
- [Confluent Kafka Golang Client](https://github.com/confluentinc/confluent-kafka-go) ⭐ 5152 - Updated Jul 2026: confluent-kafka-go is Confluent's Golang client for Apache Kafka and the Confluent Platform.
- [dbus](https://github.com/godbus/dbus) ⭐ 1184 - Updated May 2026: Native Go bindings for D-Bus.
- [drone-line](https://github.com/appleboy/drone-line) ⭐ 81 - Updated Jun 2021: Sending Line notifications using a binary, docker or Drone CI.
- [emitter](https://github.com/olebedev/emitter) ⭐ 532 - Updated Apr 2023: Emits events using Go way, with wildcard, predicates, cancellation possibilities and many other good wins.
- [event](https://github.com/agoalofalife/event) ⭐ 62 - Updated Feb 2018: Implementation of the pattern observer.
- [EventBus](https://github.com/asaskevich/EventBus) ⭐ 1980 - Updated Sep 2020: The lightweight event bus with async compatibility.
- [gaurun-client](https://github.com/osamingo/gaurun-client) ⭐ 11 - Updated Jul 2018: Gaurun Client written in Go.
- [Glue](https://github.com/desertbit/glue) ⭐ 421 - Updated Jun 2019: Robust Go and Javascript Socket Library (Alternative to Socket.io).
- [go-eventbus](https://github.com/stanipetrosyan/go-eventbus) ⭐ 11 - Updated May 2025: Simple Event Bus package for Go.
- [Go-MediatR](https://github.com/mehdihadeli/Go-MediatR) ⭐ 278 - Updated May 2025: A library for handling mediator patterns and simplified CQRS patterns within an event-driven architecture, inspired by csharp MediatR library.
- [go-mq](https://github.com/cheshir/go-mq) ⭐ 91 - Updated May 2023: RabbitMQ client with declarative configuration.
- [go-notify](https://github.com/TheCreeper/go-notify) ⭐ 71 - Updated Dec 2020: Native implementation of the freedesktop notification spec.
- [go-nsq](https://github.com/nsqio/go-nsq) ⭐ 2655 - Updated Jul 2025: the official Go package for NSQ.
- [go-res](https://github.com/jirenius/go-res) ⭐ 69 - Updated Mar 2026: Package for building REST/real-time services where clients are synchronized seamlessly, using NATS and Resgate.
- [go-vitotrol](https://github.com/maxatome/go-vitotrol) ⭐ 24 - Updated Nov 2025: Client library to Viessmann Vitotrol web service.
- [GoEventBus](https://github.com/Raezil/GoEventBus) ⭐ 68 - Updated May 2026: A blazing‑fast, in‑memory, lock‑free event bus library
- [Gollum](https://github.com/trivago/gollum) ⭐ 940 - Updated Oct 2025 - ⚠️ Archived: A n:m multiplexer that gathers messages from different sources and broadcasts them to a set of destinations.
- [golongpoll](https://github.com/jcuga/golongpoll) ⭐ 668 - Updated Aug 2023: HTTP longpoll server library that makes web pub-sub simple.
- [gopush-cluster](https://github.com/Terry-Mao/gopush-cluster) ⭐ 2071 - Updated May 2017: gopush-cluster is a go push server cluster.
- [gorush](https://github.com/appleboy/gorush) ⭐ 8749 - Updated Jul 2026: Push notification server using APNs2 and google GCM.
- [gosd](https://github.com/alexsniffin/gosd) ⭐ 26 - Updated Aug 2022: A library for scheduling when to dispatch a message to a channel.
- [guble](https://github.com/smancke/guble) ⭐ 161 - Updated Oct 2017: Messaging server using push notifications (Google Firebase Cloud Messaging, Apple Push Notification services, SMS) as well as websockets, a REST API, featuring distributed operation and message-persistence.
- [hare](https://github.com/leozz37/hare) ⭐ 55 - Updated Aug 2022: A user friendly library for sending messages and listening to TCP sockets.
- [hub](https://github.com/leandro-lugaresi/hub) ⭐ 148 - Updated Jul 2026: A Message/Event Hub for Go applications, using publish/subscribe pattern with support for alias like rabbitMQ exchanges.
- [hypermatch](https://github.com/SchwarzIT/hypermatch) ⭐ 36 - Updated May 2026: A very fast and efficient Go library for matching events to a large set of rules
- [jazz](https://github.com/socifi/jazz) ⭐ 18 - Updated Mar 2019: A simple RabbitMQ abstraction layer for queue administration and publishing and consuming of messages.
- [machinery](https://github.com/RichardKnop/machinery) ⭐ 7963 - Updated Nov 2025: Asynchronous task queue/job queue based on distributed message passing.
- [mangos](https://github.com/nanomsg/mangos) ⭐ 757 - Updated Jul 2026: Pure go implementation of the Nanomsg ("Scalability Protocols") with transport interoperability.
- [melody](https://github.com/olahol/melody) ⭐ 4080 - Updated Oct 2025: Minimalist framework for dealing with websocket sessions, includes broadcasting and automatic ping/pong handling.
- [Mercure](https://github.com/dunglas/mercure) ⭐ 5283 - Updated Jul 2026: Server and library to dispatch server-sent updates using the Mercure protocol (built on top of Server-Sent Events).
- [messagebus](https://github.com/vardius/message-bus) ⭐ 287 - Updated Jan 2021: messagebus is a Go simple async message bus, perfect for using as event bus when doing event sourcing, CQRS, DDD.
- [NATS Go Client](https://github.com/nats-io/nats.go) ⭐ 6694 - Updated Jul 2026: Go client for the NATS
- [nsq-event-bus](https://github.com/rafaeljesus/nsq-event-bus) ⭐ 80 - Updated Feb 2018: A tiny wrapper around NSQ topic and channel.
- [oplog](https://github.com/dailymotion/oplog) ⭐ 111 - Updated Sep 2024: Generic oplog/replication system for REST APIs.
- [pubsub](https://github.com/tuxychandru/pubsub) ⭐ 454 - Updated May 2024: Simple pubsub package for go.
- [Quamina](https://github.com/timbray/quamina) ⭐ 496 - Updated Jun 2026: Fast pattern-matching for filtering messages and events.
- [rabbitroutine](https://github.com/furdarius/rabbitroutine) ⭐ 115 - Updated Mar 2024: Lightweight library that handles RabbitMQ auto-reconnect and publishing retries. The library takes into account the need to re-declare entities in RabbitMQ after reconnection.
- [rabbus](https://github.com/rafaeljesus/rabbus) ⭐ 98 - Updated Jul 2019: A tiny wrapper over amqp exchanges and queues.
- [rabtap](https://github.com/jandelgado/rabtap) ⭐ 287 - Updated May 2026: RabbitMQ swiss army knife cli app.
- [RapidMQ](https://github.com/sybrexsys/RapidMQ) ⭐ 70 - Updated Dec 2017: RapidMQ is a lightweight and reliable library for managing of the local messages queue.
- [Ratus](https://github.com/hyperonym/ratus) ⭐ 124 - Updated Mar 2025: Ratus is a RESTful asynchronous task queue server.
- [redisqueue](https://github.com/robinjoseph08/redisqueue) ⭐ 138 - Updated Oct 2020: redisqueue provides a producer and consumer of a queue that uses Redis streams.
- [rmqconn](https://github.com/sbabiv/rmqconn) ⭐ 23 - Updated Jan 2020: RabbitMQ Reconnection. Wrapper over amqp.Connection and amqp.Dial. Allowing to do a reconnection when the connection is broken before forcing the call to the Close () method to be closed.
- [sarama](https://github.com/Shopify/sarama) ⭐ 12508 - Updated Jul 2026: Go library for Apache Kafka.
- [Uniqush-Push](https://github.com/uniqush/uniqush-push) ⭐ 1563 - Updated Apr 2020: Redis backed unified push service for server-side notifications to mobile devices.
- [varmq](https://github.com/goptics/varmq) ⭐ 191 - Updated Jul 2026: A storage-agnostic message queue and worker pool for concurrent Go programs.
- [Watermill](https://github.com/ThreeDotsLabs/watermill) ⭐ 9800 - Updated May 2026: Working efficiently with message streams. Building event driven applications, enabling event sourcing, RPC over messages, sagas. Can use conventional pub/sub implementations like Kafka or RabbitMQ, but also HTTP or MySQL binlog.
- [zmq4](https://github.com/pebbe/zmq4) ⭐ 1259 - Updated Jul 2025: Go interface to ZeroMQ version 4. Also available for version 3 and version 2.

## Miscellaneous
### Dependency Injection
_Libraries for working with dependency injection._

- [alice](https://github.com/magic003/alice) ⭐ 51 - Updated Apr 2017: Additive dependency injection container for Golang.
- [autowire](https://github.com/tiendc/autowire) ⭐ 12 - Updated Sep 2024: Dependency injection using Generics and reflection.
- [boot-go](http://github.com/boot-go/boot) ⭐ 36 - Updated Jan 2024: Component-based development with dependency injection using reflections for Go developers.
- [componego](https://github.com/componego/componego) ⭐ 29 - Updated Sep 2024: A dependency injection framework based on components, allowing dynamic dependency replacement without duplicating code in tests.
- [cosban/di](https://gitlab.com/cosban/di) ⭐ 1 - Updated Dec 2023: A code generation based dependency injection wiring tool.
- [di](https://github.com/goava/di) ⭐ 242 - Updated Dec 2023: A dependency injection container for go programming language.
- [dig](https://github.com/uber-go/dig) ⭐ 4487 - Updated May 2025: A reflection based dependency injection toolkit for Go.
- [dingo](https://github.com/i-love-flamingo/dingo) ⭐ 188 - Updated Jun 2026: A dependency injection toolkit for Go, based on Guice.
- [do](https://github.com/samber/do) ⭐ 2767 - Updated Jul 2026: A dependency injection framework based on Generics.
- [fx](https://github.com/uber-go/fx) ⭐ 7606 - Updated Dec 2025: A dependency injection based application framework for Go (built on top of dig).
- [go-beans](https://github.com/go-beans/go) ⭐ 1 - Updated Jul 2026: Spring-inspired dependency injection and application lifecycle framework for Go.
- [Go-Spring](https://github.com/go-spring/spring-core) ⭐ 84 - Updated May 2026 - ⚠️ Archived: A high-performance Go framework inspired by Spring Boot, offering DI, auto-configuration, and lifecycle management while maintaining Go's simplicity and efficiency.
- [gocontainer](https://github.com/vardius/gocontainer) ⭐ 21 - Updated Mar 2020: Simple Dependency Injection Container.
- [godi](https://github.com/junioryono/godi) ⭐ 75 - Updated Jul 2026: Microsoft-style dependency injection for Go with scoped lifetimes and generics.
- [goioc/di](https://github.com/goioc/di) ⭐ 379 - Updated Nov 2024: Spring-inspired Dependency Injection Container.
- [GoLobby/Container](https://github.com/golobby/container) ⭐ 614 - Updated Aug 2023: GoLobby Container is a lightweight yet powerful IoC dependency injection container for the Go programming language.
- [gontainer](https://github.com/NVIDIA/gontainer) ⭐ 153 - Updated Apr 2026: A dependency injection service container for Go projects.
- [gontainer/gontainer](https://github.com/gontainer/gontainer) ⭐ 17 - Updated Apr 2024: A YAML-based Dependency Injection container for GO. It supports dependencies' scopes, and auto-detection of circular dependencies. Gontainer is concurrent-safe.
- [HnH/di](https://github.com/HnH/di) ⭐ 9 - Updated Nov 2025: DI container library that is focused on clean API and flexibility.
- [kinit](https://github.com/go-kata/kinit) ⭐ 10 - Updated Jun 2021: Customizable dependency injection container with the global mode, cascade initialization and panic-safe finalization.
- [kod](https://github.com/go-kod/kod) ⭐ 198 - Updated Mar 2026: A generics based dependency injection framework for Go.
- [linker](https://github.com/logrange/linker) ⭐ 35 - Updated Jan 2025: A reflection based dependency injection and inversion of control library with components lifecycle support.
- [nject](https://github.com/muir/nject) ⭐ 32 - Updated Apr 2026: A type safe, reflective framework for libraries, tests, http endpoints, and service startup.
- [ore](https://github.com/firasdarwish/ore) ⭐ 27 - Updated Mar 2026: Lightweight, generic & simple dependency injection (DI) container.
- [parsley](https://github.com/matzefriedrich/parsley) ⭐ 34 - Updated Jul 2026: A flexible and modular reflection-based DI library with advanced features like scoped contexts and proxy generation, designed for large-scale Go applications.
- [wire](https://github.com/Fs02/wire) ⭐ 40 - Updated Aug 2021: Strict Runtime Dependency Injection for Golang.
### Project Layout
_Unofficial set of patterns for structuring projects._

- [ardanlabs/service](https://github.com/ardanlabs/service) ⭐ 4095 - Updated Jun 2026: A starter kit for building production grade scalable web service applications.
- [cookiecutter-golang](https://github.com/lacion/cookiecutter-golang) ⭐ 737 - Updated Oct 2023: A Go application boilerplate template for quick starting projects following production best practices.
- [go-blueprint](https://github.com/Melkeydev/go-blueprint) ⭐ 8890 - Updated Jul 2025: Allows users to spin up a quick Go project using a popular framework.
- [go-module](https://github.com/octomation/go-module) ⭐ 40 - Updated Dec 2023: Template for a typical module written on Go.
- [go-rest-api-boilerplate](https://github.com/vahiiiid/go-rest-api-boilerplate) ⭐ 60 - Updated May 2026: AI-friendly, production-ready Go REST API boilerplate with clean architecture, JWT authentication, RBAC, PostgreSQL, Docker hot-reload, and Swagger documentation.
- [go-sample](https://github.com/zitryss/go-sample) ⭐ 140 - Updated Jan 2019: A sample layout for Go application projects with the real code.
- [go-starter](https://github.com/allaboutapps/go-starter) ⭐ 618 - Updated Oct 2025: An opinionated production-ready RESTful JSON backend template, highly integrated with VSCode DevContainers.
- [go-todo-backend](https://github.com/Fs02/go-todo-backend) ⭐ 338 - Updated May 2023: Go Todo Backend example using modular project layout for product microservice.
- [goapp](https://github.com/naughtygopher/goapp) ⭐ 1068 - Updated Sep 2025: An opinionated guideline to structure & develop a Go web application/service.
- [gobase](https://github.com/wajox/gobase) ⭐ 66 - Updated Jun 2023: A simple skeleton for golang application with basic setup for real golang application.
- [golang-standards/project-layout](https://github.com/golang-standards/project-layout) ⭐ 56314 - Updated Apr 2026: Set of common historical and emerging project layout patterns in the Go ecosystem. Note: despite the org-name they do not represent official golang standards, see this issue for more information. Nonetheless, some may find the layout useful.
- [golang-templates/seed](https://github.com/golang-templates/seed) ⭐ 564 - Updated Jul 2026: Go application GitHub repository template.
- [goxygen](https://github.com/shpota/goxygen) ⭐ 3594 - Updated Dec 2024: Generate a modern Web project with Go and Angular, React, or Vue in seconds.
- [insidieux/inizio](https://github.com/insidieux/inizio) ⭐ 19 - Updated Jun 2022: Golang project layout generator with plugins.
- [kickstart.go](https://github.com/raeperd/kickstart.go) ⭐ 111 - Updated May 2026: Minimalistic single-file Go HTTP server template without third-party dependencies.
- [modern-go-application](https://github.com/sagikazarmark/modern-go-application) ⭐ 1943 - Updated Apr 2023: Go application boilerplate and example applying modern practices.
- [nunu](https://github.com/go-nunu/nunu) ⭐ 2587 - Updated Apr 2026: Nunu is a scaffolding tool for building Go applications.
- [pagoda](https://github.com/mikestefanello/pagoda) ⭐ 2945 - Updated Dec 2025: Rapid, easy full-stack web development starter kit built in Go.
- [scaffold](https://github.com/catchplay/scaffold) ⭐ 150 - Updated Jan 2019: Scaffold generates a starter Go project layout. Lets you focus on business logic implemented.
- [wangyoucao577/go-project-layout](https://github.com/wangyoucao577/go-project-layout) ⭐ 26 - Updated May 2021: Set of practices and discussions on how to structure Go project layout.
### Strings
_Libraries for working with strings._

- [bexp](https://github.com/happy-sdk/happy/tree/main/pkg/strings/bexp): Go implementation of Brace Expansion mechanism to generate arbitrary strings.
- [caps](https://github.com/chanced/caps) ⭐ 61 - Updated Dec 2023: A case conversion library.
- [go-formatter](https://gitlab.com/tymonx/go-formatter) ⭐ 10 - Updated May 2021: Implements replacement fields surrounded by curly braces {} format strings.
- [gobeam/Stringy](https://github.com/gobeam/Stringy) ⭐ 248 - Updated May 2025: String manipulation library to convert string to camel case, snake case, kebab case / slugify etc.
- [str](https://github.com/schigh/str) ⭐ 10 - Updated Mar 2026: Pipeline-first string toolkit for composing transformations.
- [strcase](https://github.com/charlievieth/strcase) ⭐ 16 - Updated Jul 2026: Case-insensitive implementation of the standard library's strings/bytes packages.
- [stringFormatter](https://github.com/Wissance/stringFormatter) ⭐ 156 - Updated Apr 2026: String formatting like in Python or C# manner with the additional text formatting features.
- [strutil](https://github.com/ozgio/strutil) ⭐ 206 - Updated Oct 2021: String utilities.

- [xstrings](https://github.com/huandu/xstrings) ⭐ 1415 - Updated Jun 2024: Collection of useful string functions ported from other languages.

## Natural Language Processing
_Libraries for working with human languages._
### Language Detection

- [detectlanguage](https://github.com/detectlanguage/detectlanguage-go) ⭐ 26 - Updated Aug 2025: Language Detection API Go Client. Supports batch requests, short phrase or single word language detection.
- [getlang](https://github.com/rylans/getlang) ⭐ 175 - Updated Dec 2020: Fast natural language detection package.
- [guesslanguage](https://github.com/endeveit/guesslanguage) ⭐ 58 - Updated Dec 2014: Functions to determine the natural language of a unicode text.
- [lingua-go](https://github.com/pemistahl/lingua-go) ⭐ 1359 - Updated Dec 2024: An accurate natural language detection library, suitable for long and short text alike. Supports detecting multiple languages in mixed-language text.
- [whatlanggo](https://github.com/abadojack/whatlanggo) ⭐ 692 - Updated Mar 2019: Natural language detection package for Go. Supports 84 languages and 24 scripts (writing systems e.g. Latin, Cyrillic, etc).
### Morphological Analyzers

- [go-stem](https://github.com/agonopol/go-stem) ⭐ 81 - Updated Jun 2015: Implementation of the porter stemming algorithm.
- [go2vec](https://github.com/danieldk/go2vec) ⭐ 58 - Updated May 2017 - ⚠️ Archived: Reader and utility functions for word2vec embeddings.
- [go-propisyu](https://github.com/rekurt/go-propisyu) ⭐ 5 - Updated May 2026: Convert numbers to Russian words with correct grammatical gender and noun declension.
- [golibstemmer](https://github.com/rjohnsondev/golibstemmer) ⭐ 21 - Updated Jun 2014: Go bindings for the snowball libstemmer library including porter 2.
- [gosentiwordnet](https://github.com/dinopuguh/gosentiwordnet) ⭐ 11 - Updated Mar 2021: Sentiment analyzer using sentiwordnet lexicon in Go.
- [govader](https://github.com/jonreiter/govader) ⭐ 55 - Updated Apr 2025: Go implementation of VADER Sentiment Analysis.
- [govader-backend](https://github.com/PIMPfiction/govader_backend) ⭐ 6 - Updated Feb 2024: Microservice implementation of GoVader.
- [kagome](https://github.com/ikawaha/kagome) ⭐ 974 - Updated Jul 2026: JP morphological analyzer written in pure Go.
- [libtextcat](https://github.com/goodsign/libtextcat) ⭐ 13 - Updated Dec 2012: Cgo binding for libtextcat C library. Guaranteed compatibility with version 2.2.
- [nlp](https://github.com/james-bowman/nlp) ⭐ 475 - Updated May 2021: Go Natural Language Processing library supporting LSA (Latent Semantic Analysis).
- [paicehusk](https://github.com/rookii/paicehusk) ⭐ 29 - Updated Jun 2013: Golang implementation of the Paice/Husk Stemming Algorithm.
- [porter](https://github.com/a2800276/porter) ⭐ 14 - Updated Feb 2026: This is a fairly straightforward port of Martin Porter's C implementation of the Porter stemming algorithm.
- [porter2](https://github.com/zhenjl/porter2) ⭐ 47 - Updated Aug 2015: Really fast Porter 2 stemmer.
- [RAKE.go](https://github.com/afjoseph/RAKE.Go) ⭐ 124 - Updated Jun 2025: Go port of the Rapid Automatic Keyword Extraction Algorithm (RAKE).
- [snowball](https://github.com/goodsign/snowball) ⭐ 38 - Updated Dec 2012: Snowball stemmer port (cgo wrapper) for Go. Provides word stem extraction functionality Snowball native.
- [spaGO](https://github.com/nlpodyssey/spago) ⭐ 1850 - Updated Apr 2025: Self-contained Machine Learning and Natural Language Processing library in Go.
- [spelling-corrector](https://github.com/jorelosorio/spellingcorrector) ⭐ 2 - Updated Mar 2022: A spelling corrector for the Spanish language or create your own.
### Slugifiers

- [go-slugify](https://github.com/mozillazg/go-slugify) ⭐ 97 - Updated Aug 2016: Make pretty slug with multiple languages support.
- [slug](https://github.com/gosimple/slug) ⭐ 1329 - Updated Dec 2024: URL-friendly slugify with multiple languages support.
- [Slugify](https://github.com/avelino/slugify) ⭐ 35 - Updated May 2018: Go slugify application that handles string.
### Tokenizers

- [gojieba](https://github.com/yanyiwu/gojieba) ⭐ 2647 - Updated Apr 2026: This is a Go implementation of jieba which a Chinese word splitting algorithm.
- [gotokenizer](https://github.com/xujiajun/gotokenizer) ⭐ 21 - Updated Apr 2019: A tokenizer based on the dictionary and Bigram language models for Golang. (Now only support chinese segmentation)
- [gse](https://github.com/go-ego/gse) ⭐ 2840 - Updated Jun 2026: Go efficient text segmentation; support english, chinese, japanese and other.
- [MMSEGO](https://github.com/awsong/MMSEGO) ⭐ 62 - Updated Apr 2012: This is a GO implementation of MMSEG which a Chinese word splitting algorithm.
- [segment](https://github.com/blevesearch/segment) ⭐ 89 - Updated Dec 2022: Go library for performing Unicode Text Segmentation as described in Unicode Standard Annex #29
- [sentences](https://github.com/neurosnap/sentences) ⭐ 473 - Updated Feb 2024: Sentence tokenizer: converts text into a list of sentences.
- [shamoji](https://github.com/osamingo/shamoji) ⭐ 13 - Updated Mar 2025: The shamoji is word filtering package written in Go.
- [stemmer](https://github.com/dchest/stemmer) ⭐ 56 - Updated Dec 2016: Stemmer packages for Go programming language. Includes English and German stemmers.
- [textcat](https://github.com/pebbe/textcat) ⭐ 73 - Updated Dec 2024: Go package for n-gram based text categorization, with support for utf-8 and raw text.
### Translation

- [ctxi18n](https://github.com/invopop/ctxi18n/) ⭐ 94 - Updated Dec 2024: Context aware i18n with a short and consise API, pluralization, interpolation, and fs.FS support. YAML locale definitions are based on Rails i18n.
- [go-i18n](https://github.com/nicksnyder/go-i18n/) ⭐ 3537 - Updated Jul 2026: Package and an accompanying tool to work with localized text.
- [go-mystem](https://github.com/dveselov/mystem) ⭐ 36 - Updated Oct 2016: CGo bindings to Yandex.Mystem - russian morphology analyzer.
- [go-pinyin](https://github.com/mozillazg/go-pinyin) ⭐ 1787 - Updated Jul 2025: CN Hanzi to Hanyu Pinyin converter.
- [go-words](https://github.com/saleh-rahimzadeh/go-words) ⭐ 8 - Updated Feb 2024: A words table and text resource library for Golang projects.
- [gotext](https://github.com/leonelquinteros/gotext) ⭐ 505 - Updated Jun 2026: GNU gettext utilities for Go.
- [iuliia-go](https://github.com/mehanizm/iuliia-go) ⭐ 57 - Updated Jan 2025: Transliterate Cyrillic → Latin in every possible way.
- [spreak](https://github.com/vorlif/spreak) ⭐ 94 - Updated Sep 2025: Flexible translation and humanization library for Go, based on the concepts behind gettext.
- [t](https://github.com/youthlin/t) ⭐ 22 - Updated Jun 2026: Another i18n pkg for golang, which follows GNU gettext style and supports .po/.mo files: t.T (gettext), t.N (ngettext), etc. And it contains a cmd tool xtemplate, which can extract messages as a pot file from text/html template.
### Transliteration

- [enca](https://github.com/endeveit/enca) ⭐ 19 - Updated Mar 2016: Minimal cgo bindings for libenca, which detects character encodings.
- [go-unidecode](https://github.com/mozillazg/go-unidecode) ⭐ 146 - Updated May 2023: ASCII transliterations of Unicode text.
- [gounidecode](https://github.com/fiam/gounidecode) ⭐ 80 - Updated Jun 2015: Unicode transliterator (also known as unidecode) for Go.
- [transliterator](https://github.com/alexsergivan/transliterator) ⭐ 46 - Updated Sep 2022: Provides one-way string transliteration with supporting of language-specific transliteration rules.

## Networking
_Libraries for working with various layers of the network._

- [arp](https://github.com/mdlayher/arp) ⭐ 391 - Updated May 2026: Package arp implements the ARP protocol, as described in RFC 826.
- [bart](https://github.com/gaissmai/bart) ⭐ 150 - Updated Jul 2026: Package bart provides a Balanced-Routing-Table (BART) for very fast IP to CIDR lookups and more.
- [buffstreams](https://github.com/stabbycutyou/buffstreams) ⭐ 255 - Updated Apr 2016: Streaming protocolbuffer data over TCP made easy.
- [canopus](https://github.com/zubairhamed/canopus) ⭐ 156 - Updated Feb 2018: CoAP Client/Server implementation (RFC 7252).
- [cdns](https://github.com/junevm/cdns) ⭐ 5 - Updated May 2026: Change DNS servers effortlessly via terminal.
- [cidranger](https://github.com/yl2chen/cidranger) ⭐ 970 - Updated Sep 2021: Fast IP to CIDR lookup for Go.
- [cloudflared](https://github.com/cloudflare/cloudflared) ⭐ 14884 - Updated Jul 2026: Cloudflare Tunnel client (formerly Argo Tunnel).
- [dhcp6](https://github.com/mdlayher/dhcp6) ⭐ 80 - Updated Mar 2019: Package dhcp6 implements a DHCPv6 server, as described in RFC 3315.
- [dns](https://github.com/miekg/dns) ⭐ 8728 - Updated Jul 2026: Go library for working with DNS.
- [dnsmonster](https://github.com/mosajjal/dnsmonster) ⭐ 357 - Updated Jul 2026: Passive DNS Capture/Monitoring Framework.
- [easytcp](https://github.com/DarthPestilane/easytcp) ⭐ 817 - Updated Jan 2026: A light-weight TCP framework written in Go (Golang), built with message router. EasyTCP helps you build a TCP server easily fast and less painful.
- [ether](https://github.com/songgao/ether) ⭐ 82 - Updated Apr 2016: Cross-platform Go package for sending and receiving ethernet frames.
- [ethernet](https://github.com/mdlayher/ethernet) ⭐ 288 - Updated Feb 2022: Package ethernet implements marshaling and unmarshalling of IEEE 802.3 Ethernet II frames and IEEE 802.1Q VLAN tags.
- [event](https://github.com/cheng-zhongliang/event) ⭐ 119 - Updated Dec 2023: Simple I/O event notification library written in Golang.
- [fasthttp](https://github.com/valyala/fasthttp) ⭐ 23414 - Updated Jul 2026: Package fasthttp is a fast HTTP implementation for Go, up to 10 times faster than net/http.
- [fortio](https://github.com/fortio/fortio) ⭐ 3708 - Updated Jul 2026: Load testing library and command line tool, advanced echo server and web UI. Allows to specify a set query-per-second load and record latency histograms and other useful stats and graph them. Tcp, Http, gRPC.
- [ftp](https://github.com/jlaffaye/ftp) ⭐ 1402 - Updated Jul 2026: Package ftp implements a FTP client as described in RFC 959.
- [ftpserverlib](https://github.com/fclairamb/ftpserverlib) ⭐ 472 - Updated Jul 2026: Fully featured FTP server library.
- [fullproxy](https://github.com/shoriwe/fullproxy) ⭐ 81 - Updated Jun 2023: A fully featured scriptable and daemon configurable proxy and pivoting toolkit with SOCKS5, HTTP, raw ports and reverse proxy protocols.
- [fwdctl](https://github.com/alegrey91/fwdctl) ⭐ 72 - Updated Jul 2026: A simple and intuitive CLI to manage IPTables forwards in your Linux server.
- [gaio](https://github.com/xtaci/gaio) ⭐ 930 - Updated Feb 2026: High performance async-io networking for Golang in proactor mode.
- [gev](https://github.com/Allenxuxu/gev) ⭐ 1775 - Updated Jun 2025: gev is a lightweight, fast non-blocking TCP network library based on Reactor mode.
- [gldap](https://github.com/jimlambrt/gldap) ⭐ 122 - Updated Aug 2024: gldap provides an ldap server implementation and you provide handlers for its ldap operations.
- [gmqtt](https://github.com/DrmagicE/gmqtt) ⭐ 1046 - Updated Apr 2026: Gmqtt is a flexible, high-performance MQTT broker library that fully implements the MQTT protocol V3.1.1.
- [gnet](https://github.com/panjf2000/gnet) ⭐ 11212 - Updated Jul 2026: gnet is a high-performance, lightweight, non-blocking, event-driven networking framework written in pure Go.
- [gnet](https://github.com/fish-tennis/gnet) ⭐ 27 - Updated Jul 2026: gnet is a high-performance networking framework,especially for game servers.
- [gNxI](https://github.com/google/gnxi) ⭐ 287 - Updated Mar 2026: A collection of tools for Network Management that use the gNMI and gNOI protocols.
- [go-getter](https://github.com/hashicorp/go-getter) ⭐ 1822 - Updated Jul 2026: Go library for downloading files or directories from various sources using a URL.
- [go-multiproxy](https://github.com/presbrey/go-multiproxy) ⭐ 29 - Updated Jul 2025: Library for making HTTP requests through a pool of proxies offering fault tolerance, load balancing, automatic retries, cookie management, and more, via http.Get/Post replacement or http.Client RoundTripper drop-in
- [go-pcaplite](https://github.com/alexcfv/go-pcaplite) ⭐ 9 - Updated May 2026: Lightweight live packet capture library with HTTPS SNI extraction.
- [go-powerdns](https://github.com/joeig/go-powerdns) ⭐ 105 - Updated Jun 2026: PowerDNS API bindings for Golang.
- [go-sse](https://github.com/lampctl/go-sse) ⭐ 15 - Updated Apr 2025: Go client and server implementation of HTML server-sent events.
- [fibersse](https://github.com/vinod-morya/fibersse) ⭐ 3 - Updated May 2026: Production-grade Server-Sent Events (SSE) for Fiber v3 with event coalescing, priority lanes, topic wildcards, adaptive throttling, and built-in auth.
- [go-stun](https://github.com/ccding/go-stun) ⭐ 721 - Updated Jan 2024: Go implementation of the STUN client (RFC 3489 and RFC 5389).
- [gobgp](https://github.com/osrg/gobgp) ⭐ 4090 - Updated Jul 2026: BGP implemented in the Go Programming Language.
- [gopacket](https://github.com/google/gopacket) ⭐ 6788 - Updated Mar 2025: Go library for packet processing with libpcap bindings.
- [gopcap](https://github.com/akrennmair/gopcap) ⭐ 491 - Updated Jul 2015: Go wrapper for libpcap.
- [GoProxy](https://github.com/elazarl/goproxy) ⭐ 6709 - Updated Jul 2026: A library to create a customized HTTP/HTTPS proxy server using Go.
- [goshark](https://github.com/sunwxg/goshark) ⭐ 18 - Updated Oct 2017: Package goshark use tshark to decode IP packet and create data struct to analyse packet.
- [gosnmp](https://github.com/soniah/gosnmp) ⭐ 1 - Updated Apr 2026: Native Go library for performing SNMP actions.
- [gotcp](https://github.com/gansidui/gotcp) ⭐ 511 - Updated Apr 2017: Go package for quickly writing tcp applications.
- [grab](https://github.com/cavaliercoder/grab) ⭐ 1480 - Updated Jan 2022: Go package for managing file downloads.
- [graval](https://github.com/koofr/graval) ⭐ 28 - Updated Oct 2020: Experimental FTP server framework.
- [gws](https://github.com/lxzan/gws) ⭐ 1793 - Updated Jul 2026: High-Performance WebSocket Server & Client With AsyncIO Supporting .
- [HTTPLab](https://github.com/gchaincl/httplab) ⭐ 4150 - Updated Feb 2024: HTTPLabs let you inspect HTTP requests and forge responses.
- [httpproxy](https://github.com/wzshiming/httpproxy) ⭐ 33 - Updated Jul 2026: HTTP proxy handler and dialer.
- [iplib](https://github.com/c-robinson/iplib) ⭐ 151 - Updated Apr 2024: Library for working with IP addresses (net.IP, net.IPNet), inspired by python ipaddress and ruby ipaddr
- [jazigo](https://github.com/udhos/jazigo) ⭐ 230 - Updated Nov 2023: Jazigo is a tool written in Go for retrieving configuration for multiple network devices.
- [kcp-go](https://github.com/xtaci/kcp-go) ⭐ 4532 - Updated May 2026: KCP - Fast and Reliable ARQ Protocol.
- [kcptun](https://github.com/xtaci/kcptun): Extremely simple & fast udp tunnel based on KCP protocol.
- [lhttp](https://github.com/fanux/lhttp) ⭐ 688 - Updated Apr 2018: Powerful websocket framework, build your IM server more easily.
- [linkio](https://github.com/ian-kent/linkio) ⭐ 53 - Updated Aug 2017: Network link speed simulation for Reader/Writer interfaces.
- [llb](https://github.com/kirillDanshin/llb) ⭐ 16 - Updated Apr 2016: It's a very simple but quick backend for proxy servers. Can be useful for fast redirection to predefined domain with zero memory allocation and fast response.
- [macwifi](https://github.com/jaisonerick/macwifi) ⭐ 7 - Updated Apr 2026: Wi-Fi scanning and Keychain password retrieval for macOS 13+.
- [mdns](https://github.com/hashicorp/mdns) ⭐ 1366 - Updated Jul 2026: Simple mDNS (Multicast DNS) client/server library in Golang.
- [mqttPaho](https://eclipse.org/paho/clients/golang/): The Paho Go Client provides an MQTT client library for connection to MQTT brokers via TCP, TLS or WebSockets.
- [natiu-mqtt](https://github.com/soypat/natiu-mqtt) ⭐ 106 - Updated Jun 2026: A dead-simple, non-allocating, low level implementation of MQTT well suited for embedded systems.
- [nbio](https://github.com/lesismal/nbio) ⭐ 2753 - Updated Jul 2026: Pure Go 1000k+ connections solution, support tls/http1.x/websocket and basically compatible with net/http, with high-performance and low memory cost, non-blocking, event-driven, easy-to-use.
- [net](https://golang.org/x/net): This repository holds supplementary Go networking libraries.
- [netpoll](https://github.com/cloudwego/netpoll) ⭐ 4593 - Updated Jun 2026: A high-performance non-blocking I/O networking framework, which focused on RPC scenarios, developed by ByteDance.
- [NFF-Go](https://github.com/intel-go/nff-go) ⭐ 1420 - Updated Nov 2022: Framework for rapid development of performant network functions for cloud and bare-metal (former YANFF).
- [nodepass](https://github.com/NodePassProject/nodepass) ⭐ 268 - Updated Jul 2026: A secure, efficient TCP/UDP tunneling solution that delivers fast, reliable access across network restrictions using pre-established TCP/QUIC/WebSocket or HTTP/2 connections.
- [peerdiscovery](https://github.com/schollz/peerdiscovery) ⭐ 671 - Updated Jan 2025: Pure Go library for cross-platform local peer discovery using UDP multicast.
- [portproxy](https://github.com/aybabtme/portproxy) ⭐ 58 - Updated Dec 2014: Simple TCP proxy which adds CORS support to API's which don't support it.
- [psql-wire](https://github.com/jeroenrinzema/psql-wire) ⭐ 238 - Updated Apr 2026: PostgreSQL server wire protocol. Build your own server and start serving connections..
- [publicip](https://github.com/polera/publicip) ⭐ 29 - Updated Dec 2016: Package publicip returns your public facing IPv4 address (internet egress).
- [quic-go](https://github.com/lucas-clemente/quic-go) ⭐ 11707 - Updated Jul 2026: An implementation of the QUIC protocol in pure Go.
- [sdns](https://github.com/semihalev/sdns) ⭐ 1067 - Updated Jul 2026: A high-performance, recursive DNS resolver server with DNSSEC support, focused on preserving privacy.
- [sftp](https://github.com/pkg/sftp) ⭐ 1661 - Updated Jul 2026: Package sftp implements the SSH File Transfer Protocol as described in <https://filezilla-project.org/specs/draft-ietf-secsh-filexfer-02.txt>.
- [ssh](https://github.com/gliderlabs/ssh) ⭐ 4157 - Updated Jan 2025: Higher-level API for building SSH servers (wraps crypto/ssh).
- [sslb](https://github.com/eduardonunesp/sslb) ⭐ 152 - Updated Feb 2024: It's a Super Simples Load Balancer, just a little project to achieve some kind of performance.
- [stun](https://github.com/go-rtc/stun) ⭐ 495 - Updated Nov 2020 - ⚠️ Archived: Go implementation of RFC 5389 STUN protocol.
- [tcpack](https://github.com/lim-yoona/tcpack) ⭐ 164 - Updated Oct 2023: tcpack is an application protocol based on TCP to Pack and Unpack bytes stream in go program.
- [tspool](https://github.com/two/tspool) ⭐ 14 - Updated Oct 2018: A TCP Library use worker pool to improve performance and protect your server.
- [tun2socks](https://github.com/xjasonlyu/tun2socks) ⭐ 5405 - Updated Jul 2026: A pure go implementation of tun2socks powered by gVisor TCP/IP stack.
- [utp](https://github.com/anacrolix/utp) ⭐ 183 - Updated May 2023: Go uTP micro transport protocol implementation.
- [vssh](https://github.com/yahoo/vssh) ⭐ 991 - Updated Nov 2020: Go library for building network and server automation over SSH protocol.
- [water](https://github.com/songgao/water) ⭐ 2164 - Updated Mar 2020: Simple TUN/TAP library.
- [webrtc](https://github.com/pions/webrtc) ⭐ 16640 - Updated Jul 2026: A pure Go implementation of the WebRTC API.
- [winrm](https://github.com/masterzen/winrm) ⭐ 475 - Updated Apr 2026: Go WinRM client to remotely execute commands on Windows machines.
- [xtcp](https://github.com/xfxdev/xtcp) ⭐ 160 - Updated Feb 2020: TCP Server Framework with simultaneous full duplex communication, graceful shutdown, and custom protocol.
### HTTP Clients
_Libraries for making HTTP requests._

- [axios4go](https://github.com/rezmoss/axios4go) ⭐ 38 - Updated Jul 2026: A Go HTTP client library inspired by Axios, providing a simple and intuitive API for making HTTP requests.
- [azuretls-client](https://github.com/Noooste/azuretls-client) ⭐ 464 - Updated Apr 2026: An easy-to-use HTTP client 100% in Go to spoof TLS/JA3 and HTTP2 fingerprint.
- [fast-shot](https://github.com/opus-domini/fast-shot) ⭐ 125 - Updated Jul 2026: Hit your API targets with rapid-fire precision using Go's fastest and simple HTTP Client.
- [gentleman](https://github.com/h2non/gentleman) ⭐ 1131 - Updated Dec 2023: Full-featured plugin-driven HTTP client library.
- [go-cleanhttp](https://github.com/hashicorp/go-cleanhttp) ⭐ 442 - Updated Jul 2026: Get easily stdlib HTTP client, which does not share any state with other clients.
- [go-http-client](https://github.com/bozd4g/go-http-client) ⭐ 84 - Updated Jan 2024: Make http calls simply and easily.
- [go-ipmux](https://github.com/optimus-hft/go-ipmux) ⭐ 28 - Updated Mar 2024: A library for Multiplexing HTTP requests based on multiple Source IPs.
- [go-otelroundtripper](https://github.com/NdoleStudio/go-otelroundtripper) ⭐ 88 - Updated Jun 2026: Go http.RoundTripper that emits open telemetry metrics for HTTP requests.
- [go-req](https://github.com/wenerme/go-req) ⭐ 24 - Updated Mar 2026: Declarative golang HTTP client.
- [go-retryablehttp](https://github.com/hashicorp/go-retryablehttp) ⭐ 2339 - Updated Apr 2026: Retryable HTTP client in Go.
- [go-zoox/fetch](https://github.com/go-zoox/fetch) ⭐ 91 - Updated Jan 2026: A Powerful, Lightweight, Easy Http Client, inspired by Web Fetch API.
- [Grequest](https://github.com/lib4u/grequest) ⭐ 9 - Updated Jan 2025: Simple and lightweight golang package for http requests. based on powerful net/http
- [grequests](https://github.com/levigross/grequests) ⭐ 2187 - Updated Jun 2025: A Go "clone" of the great and famous Requests library.
- [hedge](https://github.com/bhope/hedge) ⭐ 286 - Updated May 2026: Adaptive hedged requests for Go. Cuts p99 latency with zero configuration, based on Google's "The Tail at Scale" paper.
- [heimdall](https://github.com/gojektech/heimdall) ⭐ 2774 - Updated Jul 2026: An enhanced http client with retry and hystrix capabilities.
- [httpretry](https://github.com/ybbus/httpretry) ⭐ 56 - Updated Feb 2023: Enriches the default go HTTP client with retry functionality.
- [pester](https://github.com/sethgrid/pester) ⭐ 655 - Updated Feb 2022: Go HTTP client calls with retries, backoff, and concurrency.
- [req](https://github.com/imroc/req) ⭐ 4823 - Updated Jul 2026: Simple Go HTTP client with Black Magic (Less code and More efficiency).
- [request](https://github.com/monaco-io/request) ⭐ 296 - Updated Nov 2025: HTTP client for golang. If you have experience about axios or requests, you will love it. No 3rd dependency.
- [requests](https://github.com/carlmjohnson/requests) ⭐ 1672 - Updated Jul 2026: HTTP requests for Gophers. Uses context.Context and doesn't hide the underlying net/http.Client, making it compatible with standard Go APIs. Also includes testing tools.
- [resty](https://github.com/go-resty/resty) ⭐ 11728 - Updated Jul 2026: Simple HTTP and REST client for Go inspired by Ruby rest-client.
- [rq](https://github.com/ddo/rq) ⭐ 52 - Updated Aug 2019: A nicer interface for golang stdlib HTTP client.
- [sling](https://github.com/dghubble/sling) ⭐ 1720 - Updated Mar 2026: Sling is a Go HTTP client library for creating and sending API requests.
- [surf](https://github.com/enetx/surf) ⭐ 1771 - Updated Jul 2026: Advanced HTTP client with HTTP/1.1, HTTP/2, HTTP/3 (QUIC), SOCKS5 proxy support and browser-grade TLS fingerprinting.
- [tls-client](https://github.com/bogdanfinn/tls-client) ⭐ 1734 - Updated Jul 2026: net/http.Client like HTTP Client with options to select specific client TLS Fingerprints to use for requests.

## ORM
_Libraries that implement Object-Relational Mapping or datamapping techniques._

- [bob](https://github.com/stephenafamo/bob) ⭐ 1744 - Updated Jul 2026: SQL query builder and ORM/Factory generator for Go. Successor of SQLBoiler.
- [bun](https://github.com/uptrace/bun) ⭐ 4887 - Updated Jul 2026: SQL-first Golang ORM. Successor of go-pg.
- [cacheme](https://github.com/Yiling-J/cacheme-go) ⭐ 25 - Updated Dec 2021: Schema based, typed Redis caching/memoize framework for Go.
- [CQL](https://github.com/FrancoLiberali/cql) ⭐ 18 - Updated Nov 2025: Built on top of GORM, adds compile-time verified queries based on auto-generated code.
- [ent](https://github.com/facebook/ent) ⭐ 17138 - Updated May 2026: An entity framework for Go. Simple, yet powerful ORM for modeling and querying data.
- [go-dbw](https://github.com/hashicorp/go-dbw) ⭐ 18 - Updated Jul 2026: A simple package that encapsulates database operations.
- [go-firestorm](https://github.com/jschoedt/go-firestorm) ⭐ 53 - Updated Dec 2021: A simple ORM for Google/Firebase Cloud Firestore.
- [go-sql](https://github.com/rushteam/gosql) ⭐ 177 - Updated Jun 2021: A easy ORM for mysql.
- [go-sqlbuilder](https://github.com/huandu/go-sqlbuilder) ⭐ 1718 - Updated Jun 2026: A flexible and powerful SQL string builder library plus a zero-config ORM.
- [go-store](https://github.com/gosuri/go-store) ⭐ 113 - Updated Feb 2017: Simple and fast Redis backed key-value store library for Go.
- [golobby/orm](https://github.com/golobby/orm) ⭐ 163 - Updated Jun 2026: Simple, fast, type-safe, generic orm for developer happiness.
- [GORM](https://github.com/go-gorm/gorm) ⭐ 39870 - Updated Jun 2026: The fantastic ORM library for Golang, aims to be developer friendly.
- [gormt](https://github.com/xxjwxc/gormt) ⭐ 2428 - Updated Feb 2026: Mysql database to golang gorm struct.
- [gorp](https://github.com/go-gorp/gorp) ⭐ 3751 - Updated Nov 2024: Go Relational Persistence, ORM-ish library for Go.
- [grimoire](https://github.com/Fs02/grimoire) ⭐ 161 - Updated Oct 2021: Grimoire is a database access layer and validation for golang. (Support: MySQL, PostgreSQL and SQLite3).
- [lore](https://github.com/abrahambotros/lore) ⭐ 14 - Updated Oct 2017: Simple and lightweight pseudo-ORM/pseudo-struct-mapping environment for Go.
- [marlow](https://github.com/marlow/marlow) ⭐ 12 - Updated Aug 2020: Generated ORM from project structs for compile time safety assurances.
- [pop/soda](https://github.com/gobuffalo/pop) ⭐ 1515 - Updated Jul 2026: Database migration, creation, ORM, etc... for MySQL, PostgreSQL, and SQLite.
- [Prisma](https://github.com/prisma/prisma-client-go) ⭐ 2280 - Updated Jun 2025 - ⚠️ Archived: Prisma Client Go, Typesafe database access for Go.
- [reform](https://github.com/go-reform/reform) ⭐ 1457 - Updated Jan 2022: Better ORM for Go, based on non-empty interfaces and code generation.
- [rel](https://github.com/go-rel/rel) ⭐ 785 - Updated May 2026: Modern Database Access Layer for Golang - Testable, Extendable and Crafted Into a Clean and Elegant API.
- [SQLBoiler](https://github.com/volatiletech/sqlboiler) ⭐ 6989 - Updated Jul 2026: ORM generator. Generate a featureful and blazing-fast ORM tailored to your database schema.
- [upper.io/db](https://github.com/upper/db) ⭐ 3662 - Updated Dec 2025: Single interface for interacting with different data sources through the use of adapters that wrap mature database drivers.
- [XORM](https://gitea.com/xorm/xorm): Simple and powerful ORM for Go. (Support: MySQL, MyMysql, PostgreSQL, Tidb, SQLite3, MsSql and Oracle).
- [Zoom](https://github.com/albrow/zoom) ⭐ 311 - Updated Feb 2023: Blazing-fast datastore and querying engine built on Redis.

- [modup](https://github.com/chaindead/modup) ⭐ 65 - Updated Aug 2025: Terminal UI for Go dependency updates with outdated module detection and selective upgrading.
- [syft](https://github.com/anchore/syft) ⭐ 9251 - Updated Jul 2026: A CLI tool and Go library for generating a Software Bill of Materials (SBOM) from container images and filesystems.

## Science and Data Analysis

- [gograph](https://github.com/hmdsefi/gograph) ⭐ 123 - Updated Sep 2025: A golang generic graph library that provides mathematical graph-theory and algorithms.
- [gonum](https://github.com/gonum/gonum) ⭐ 8414 - Updated May 2026: Gonum is a set of numeric libraries for the Go programming language. It contains libraries for matrices, statistics, optimization, and more.
- [gonum/plot](https://github.com/gonum/plot) ⭐ 2961 - Updated Apr 2026: gonum/plot provides an API for building and drawing plots in Go.
- [goraph](https://github.com/gyuho/goraph) ⭐ 748 - Updated Apr 2022: Pure Go graph theory library(data structure, algorithm visualization).
- [gosl](https://github.com/cpmech/gosl) ⭐ 1877 - Updated Dec 2025: Go scientific library for linear algebra, FFT, geometry, NURBS, numerical methods, probabilities, optimisation, differential equations, and more.
- [GoStats](https://github.com/OGFris/GoStats) ⭐ 22 - Updated Jan 2019: GoStats is an Open Source GoLang library for math statistics mostly used in Machine Learning domains, it covers most of the Statistical measures functions.

- [hdf5](https://github.com/scigolib/hdf5) ⭐ 28 - Updated Jun 2026: Pure Go implementation of the HDF5 file format for scientific data storage and exchange.

- [matrix](https://github.com/Arceus-7/matrix) ⭐ 7 - Updated May 2026: A clean, generic, zero-dependency matrix math package for Go with support for arithmetic, decompositions, and linear system solving.
- [ode](https://github.com/ChristopherRabotin/ode) ⭐ 22 - Updated Jan 2017: Ordinary differential equation (ODE) solver which supports extended states and channel-based iteration stop conditions.
- [orb](https://github.com/paulmach/orb) ⭐ 1122 - Updated Mar 2026: 2D geometry types with clipping, GeoJSON and Mapbox Vector Tile support.

- [PiHex](https://github.com/claygod/PiHex) ⭐ 21 - Updated Apr 2026: Implementation of the "Bailey-Borwein-Plouffe" algorithm for the hexadecimal number Pi.
- [Poly](https://github.com/bebop/poly) ⭐ 731 - Updated Jun 2026: A Go package for engineering organisms.
- [rootfinding](https://github.com/khezen/rootfinding) ⭐ 12 - Updated Mar 2020: root-finding algorithms library for finding roots of quadratic functions.
- [sparse](https://github.com/james-bowman/sparse) ⭐ 170 - Updated Feb 2026: Go Sparse matrix formats for linear algebra supporting scientific and machine learning applications, compatible with gonum matrix libraries.
- [stats](https://github.com/montanaflynn/stats) ⭐ 3022 - Updated Jul 2026: Statistics package with common functions missing from the Golang standard library.
- [streamtools](https://github.com/nytlabs/streamtools) ⭐ 1311 - Updated Apr 2015: general purpose, graphical tool for dealing with streams of data.
- [taxonkit](https://github.com/shenwei356/taxonkit) ⭐ 475 - Updated Jul 2026: A practical and efficient NCBI taxonomy toolkit; supports querying lineage, reformatting, filtering, and creating custom taxdump files.
- [TextRank](https://github.com/DavidBelicza/TextRank) ⭐ 225 - Updated Jun 2025: TextRank implementation in Golang with extendable features (summarization, weighting, phrase extraction) and multithreading (goroutine) support.
- [topk](https://github.com/keilerkonzept/topk) ⭐ 19 - Updated Apr 2025: Sliding-window and regular top-K sketches, based on the HeavyKeeper algorithm.
- [triangolatte](https://github.com/tchayen/triangolatte) ⭐ 37 - Updated Aug 2021: 2D triangulation library. Allows translating lines and polygons (both based on points) to the language of GPUs.
