## Security
_Libraries that are used to help make your application more secure._

- [acmetool](https://github.com/hlandau/acme) ⭐ 2091 - Updated Jan 2023: ACME (Let's Encrypt) client tool with automatic renewal.
- [acopw-go](https://sr.ht/~jamesponddotco/acopw-go/): Small cryptographically secure password generator package for Go.
- [acra](https://github.com/cossacklabs/acra) ⭐ 1485 - Updated Dec 2025: Network encryption proxy to protect database-based applications from data leaks: strong selective encryption, SQL injections prevention, intrusion detection system.
- [aes-ctr-drbg](https://github.com/sixafter/aes-ctr-drbg) ⭐ 9 - Updated Jun 2026: A Deterministic Random Bit Generator based on AES in Counter mode (AES-CTR-DRBG) as specified in NIST SP 800-90A.
- [age](https://github.com/FiloSottile/age) ⭐ 22903 - Updated Mar 2026: A simple, modern and secure encryption tool (and Go library) with small explicit keys, no config options, and UNIX-style composability.
- [argon2-hashing](https://github.com/andskur/argon2-hashing) ⭐ 25 - Updated May 2025: light wrapper around Go's argon2 package that closely mirrors with Go's standard library Bcrypt and simple-scrypt package.
- [autocert](https://pkg.go.dev/golang.org/x/crypto/acme/autocert): Auto provision Let's Encrypt certificates and start a TLS server.
- [BadActor](https://github.com/jaredfolkins/badactor) ⭐ 326 - Updated May 2020: In-memory, application-driven jailer built in the spirit of fail2ban.
- [beelzebub](https://github.com/mariocandela/beelzebub) ⭐ 2091 - Updated Jul 2026: A secure low code honeypot framework, leveraging AI for System Virtualization.
- [booster](https://github.com/anatol/booster) ⭐ 658 - Updated Jul 2026: Fast initramfs generator with full-disk encryption support.
- [canery](https://github.com/rluders/canery) ⭐ 8 - Updated Jun 2026: Minimal, stateless authorization engine with a pluggable evaluation model.
- [Cameradar](https://github.com/Ullaakut/cameradar) ⭐ 5126 - Updated Jul 2026: Tool and library to remotely hack RTSP streams from surveillance cameras.
- [certificates](https://github.com/mvmaasakkers/certificates) ⭐ 38 - Updated Dec 2022: An opinionated tool for generating tls certificates.
- [CertMagic](https://github.com/caddyserver/certmagic) ⭐ 5583 - Updated Jul 2026: Mature, robust, and powerful ACME client integration for fully-managed TLS certificate issuance and renewal.
- [Coraza](https://github.com/corazawaf/coraza) ⭐ 3665 - Updated Jul 2026: Enterprise-ready, modsecurity and OWASP CRS compatible WAF library.
- [dongle](https://github.com/golang-module/dongle) ⭐ 1108 - Updated May 2026: A simple, semantic and developer-friendly golang package for encoding&decoding and encryption&decryption.
- [dotlock](https://github.com/ahmadraza100/dotlock) ⭐ 4 - Updated May 2026: Encrypted .env vault manager with interactive TUI for managing secrets across multiple environments and profiles.
- [encid](https://github.com/bobg/encid) ⭐ 7 - Updated Apr 2026: Encode and decode encrypted integer IDs.
- [entpassgen](https://github.com/andreimerlescu/entpassgen) ⭐ 7 - Updated Apr 2026: Entropy Password Generator with extensive command line arguments to generate random strings securely including digits, passwords, and passwords built using obscure dictionary words mixed with symbols and digits.
- [firewalld-rest](https://github.com/prashantgupta24/firewalld-rest) ⭐ 344 - Updated Sep 2020: A rest application to dynamically update firewalld rules on a linux server.
- [fort](https://github.com/djadmin/fort) ⭐ 72 - Updated Jul 2026: Audits macOS security settings across 16 checks, reports a score, and fixes issues where it safely can. Single binary, installable via Homebrew.
- [go-generate-password](https://github.com/m1/go-generate-password) ⭐ 57 - Updated Apr 2022: Password generator that can be used on the cli or as a library.
- [go-htpasswd](https://github.com/tg123/go-htpasswd) ⭐ 49 - Updated Jun 2026: Apache htpasswd Parser for Go.
- [go-password-validator](https://github.com/lane-c-wagner/go-password-validator) ⭐ 583 - Updated Aug 2022: Password validator based on raw cryptographic entropy values.
- [go-peer](https://github.com/number571/go-peer) ⭐ 327 - Updated Jun 2026: A software library for creating secure and anonymous decentralized systems.
- [go-yara](https://github.com/hillu/go-yara) ⭐ 389 - Updated Jul 2025: Go Bindings for YARA, the "pattern matching swiss knife for malware researchers (and everyone else)".
- [goArgonPass](https://github.com/dwin/goArgonPass) ⭐ 20 - Updated Dec 2020 - ⚠️ Archived: Argon2 password hash and verification designed to be compatible with existing Python and PHP implementations.
- [goSecretBoxPassword](https://github.com/dwin/goSecretBoxPassword) ⭐ 60 - Updated Aug 2022: A probably paranoid package for securely hashing and encrypting passwords.
- [gost-crypto](https://github.com/rekurt/gost-crypto) ⭐ 2 - Updated Apr 2026: Go library for Russian GOST cryptographic standards (digital signatures, Streebog hash, Kuznechik cipher, MGM AEAD) backed by OpenSSL gost-engine.
- [gspy](https://github.com/Mutasem-mk4/gspy) ⭐ 1 - Updated Apr 2026: Forensic goroutine-to-syscall inspector for live Go processes.
- [Interpol](https://github.com/avahidi/interpol) ⭐ 7 - Updated Jul 2025: Rule-based data generator for fuzzing and penetration testing.
- [leakhound](https://github.com/nilpoona/leakhound) ⭐ 17 - Updated Jun 2026: Static analysis tool to detect accidental logging of sensitive struct fields, preventing data leaks in logs.
- [lego](https://github.com/go-acme/lego) ⭐ 9746 - Updated Jul 2026: Pure Go ACME client library and CLI tool (for use with Let's Encrypt).
- [luks.go](https://github.com/anatol/luks.go) ⭐ 98 - Updated Jun 2026: Pure Golang library to manage LUKS partitions.
- [memguard](https://github.com/awnumar/memguard) ⭐ 2751 - Updated May 2026: A pure Go library for handling sensitive values in memory.
- [multikey](https://github.com/adrianosela/multikey) ⭐ 13 - Updated May 2024: An n-out-of-N keys encryption/decryption framework based on Shamir's Secret Sharing algorithm.
- [nacl](https://github.com/kevinburke/nacl) ⭐ 553 - Updated May 2026: Go implementation of the NaCL set of API's.
- [optimus-go](https://github.com/pjebs/optimus-go) ⭐ 369 - Updated May 2020: ID hashing and Obfuscation using Knuth's Algorithm.
- [passlib](https://github.com/hlandau/passlib) ⭐ 289 - Updated Mar 2021: Futureproof password hashing library.
- [passwap](https://github.com/zitadel/passwap) ⭐ 77 - Updated Jul 2026: Provides a unified implementation between different password hashing algorithms
- [pii-shield](https://github.com/aragossa/pii-shield) ⭐ 161 - Updated Jul 2026: Zero-code log sanitization sidecar for Kubernetes that redacts PII from logs.
- [pm](https://github.com/nicola-strappazzon/password-manager) ⭐ 2 - Updated Jul 2026: Unix-style password manager written in Go to save your data with OpenPGP encryption.
- [procscope](https://github.com/Mutasem-mk4/procscope) ⭐ 23 - Updated Jun 2026: Process-scoped runtime investigator using eBPF to trace process lifecycle, file activity, and network connections.
- [qrand](https://github.com/bitfield/qrand) ⭐ 18 - Updated Feb 2024: Client for the ANU Quantum Numbers (AQN) API, providing quantum-mechanically secure random data.
- [Razify](https://github.com/Hossiy21/razify) ⭐ 20 - Updated May 2026: CLI to scan, validate and audit .env files for leaked secrets and environment drift.
- [redact](https://github.com/alesr/redact) ⭐ 2 - Updated Apr 2026: Redact sensitive information from slog-based logs using a configurable pipeline.
- [SafeDep/vet](https://github.com/safedep/vet) ⭐ 1092 - Updated Jul 2026: Protect against malicious open source packages.
- [secret](https://github.com/rsjethani/secret) ⭐ 33 - Updated Aug 2024: Prevent your secrets from leaking into logs, std\* etc.
- [secure](https://github.com/unrolled/secure) ⭐ 2348 - Updated May 2026: HTTP middleware for Go that facilitates some quick security wins.
- [secureio](https://github.com/xaionaro-go/secureio) ⭐ 33 - Updated Jul 2025 - ⚠️ Archived: An keyexchanging+authenticating+encrypting wrapper and multiplexer for io.ReadWriteCloser based on XChaCha20-poly1305, ECDH and ED25519.
- [simple-scrypt](https://github.com/elithrar/simple-scrypt) ⭐ 203 - Updated Feb 2026: Scrypt package with a simple, obvious API and automatic cost calibration built-in.
- [ssh-vault](https://github.com/ssh-vault/ssh-vault) ⭐ 507 - Updated Jul 2026: encrypt/decrypt using ssh keys.
- [sslmgr](https://github.com/adrianosela/sslmgr) ⭐ 32 - Updated Jun 2025: SSL certificates made easy with a high level wrapper around acme/autocert.
- [teler-waf](https://github.com/kitabisa/teler-waf) ⭐ 402 - Updated Feb 2025: teler-waf is a Go HTTP middleware that provide teler IDS functionality to protect against web-based attacks and improve the security of Go-based web applications. It is highly configurable and easy to integrate into existing Go applications.
- [themis](https://github.com/cossacklabs/themis) ⭐ 1968 - Updated Sep 2024: high-level cryptographic library for solving typical data security tasks (secure data storage, secure messaging, zero-knowledge proof authentication), available for 14 languages, best fit for multi-platform apps.
- [urusai](https://github.com/calpa/urusai) ⭐ 180 - Updated Jun 2026: Urusai ("noisy" in Japanese) is a Go implementation of a random HTTP/DNS traffic noise generator that helps protect privacy by creating digital smokescreens while browsing.
- [veil](https://github.com/getveil/veil) ⭐ 8 - Updated May 2026: Local HTTPS proxy that hides API credentials from AI coding agents. OS keychain integration, format-aware placeholders, SQLite audit log.

- [fwencoder](https://github.com/o1egl/fwencoder) ⭐ 27 - Updated Feb 2025: Fixed width file parser (encoding and decoding library) for Go.

- [go-csvlib](https://github.com/tiendc/go-csvlib) ⭐ 18 - Updated Sep 2024: High level and rich functionalities CSV serialization/deserialization library.
- [goprotobuf](https://github.com/golang/protobuf) ⭐ 10083 - Updated Mar 2024: Go support, in the form of a library and protocol compiler plugin, for Google's protocol buffers.
- [gotiny](https://github.com/raszia/gotiny) ⭐ 21 - Updated Jan 2024: Efficient Go serialization library, gotiny is almost as fast as serialization libraries that generate code.
- [jsoniter](https://github.com/json-iterator/go) ⭐ 13895 - Updated Sep 2022 - ⚠️ Archived: High-performance 100% compatible drop-in replacement of "encoding/json".
- [mus-go](https://github.com/mus-format/mus-go) ⭐ 144 - Updated May 2026: MUS format serializer for Go.
- [php_session_decoder](https://github.com/yvasiyarov/php_session_decoder) ⭐ 170 - Updated Aug 2018: GoLang library for working with PHP session format and PHP Serialize/Unserialize functions.
- [pletter](https://github.com/vimeda/pletter) ⭐ 20 - Updated Mar 2023: A standard way to wrap a proto message for message brokers.
- [proto](https://github.com/emicklei/proto) ⭐ 616 - Updated Feb 2026: Parser and writer for Google ProtocolBuffers .proto files.
- [structomap](https://github.com/tuvistavie/structomap) ⭐ 145 - Updated May 2019: Library to easily and dynamically generate maps from static structures.
- [unitpacking](https://github.com/recolude/unitpacking) ⭐ 7 - Updated Apr 2021: Library to pack unit vectors into as fewest bytes as possible.

## Template Engines
_Libraries and tools for templating and lexing._

- [bagme](https://github.com/boxesandglue/bagme) ⭐ 106 - Updated Jul 2026: HTML/CSS to PDF rendering with TeX-quality typesetting in pure Go.
- [ego](https://github.com/benbjohnson/ego) ⭐ 590 - Updated Jul 2021: Lightweight templating language that lets you write templates in Go. Templates are translated into Go and compiled.
- [fasttemplate](https://github.com/valyala/fasttemplate) ⭐ 909 - Updated Oct 2022: Simple and fast template engine. Substitutes template placeholders up to 10x faster than text/template.
- [gomponents](https://www.gomponents.com): HTML 5 components in pure Go, that look something like this: func(name string) g.Node { return Div(Class("headline"), g.Textf("Hi %v!", name)) }.
- [got](https://github.com/goradd/got) ⭐ 38 - Updated Jan 2026: A Go code generator inspired by Hero and Fasttemplate. Has include files, custom tag definitions, injected Go code, language translation, and more.
- [goview](https://github.com/foolin/goview) ⭐ 463 - Updated Mar 2023: Goview is a lightweight, minimalist and idiomatic template library based on golang html/template for building Go web application.
- [gox](https://github.com/doors-dev/gox) ⭐ 59 - Updated Jul 2026: HTML templates as first-class Go expressions, with seamless editor support.
- [htmgo](https://htmgo.dev): build simple and scalable systems with go + htmx
- [jet](https://github.com/CloudyKit/jet) ⭐ 1404 - Updated Jun 2026: Jet template engine.
- [liquid](https://github.com/osteele/liquid) ⭐ 355 - Updated Feb 2026: Go implementation of Shopify Liquid templates.
- [maroto](https://github.com/johnfercher/maroto) ⭐ 2739 - Updated Apr 2026: A maroto way to create PDFs. Maroto is inspired in Bootstrap and uses gofpdf. Fast and simple.
- [pongo2](https://github.com/flosch/pongo2) ⭐ 3077 - Updated Mar 2026: Django-like template-engine for Go.
- [quicktemplate](https://github.com/valyala/quicktemplate) ⭐ 3326 - Updated Jul 2024: Fast, powerful, yet easy to use template engine. Converts templates into Go code and then compiles it.
- [Razor](https://github.com/sipin/gorazor) ⭐ 884 - Updated Jun 2026: Razor view engine for Golang.
- [Soy](https://github.com/robfig/soy) ⭐ 177 - Updated Mar 2024: Closure templates (aka Soy templates) for Go, following the official spec.
- [sprout](https://github.com/go-sprout/sprout) ⭐ 225 - Updated Mar 2026: Useful template functions for Go templates.
- [tbd](https://github.com/lucasepe/tbd) ⭐ 26 - Updated Aug 2021: A really simple way to create text templates with placeholders - exposes extra builtin Git repo metadata.
- [templ](https://github.com/a-h/templ) ⭐ 10413 - Updated Jul 2026: A HTML templating language that has great developer tooling.
- [templator](https://github.com/alesr/templator) ⭐ 11 - Updated Apr 2026: A type-safe HTML template rendering engine for Go.

## Testing
_Libraries for testing codebases and generating test data._
### Testing Frameworks

- [apitest](https://apitest.dev): Simple and extensible behavioural testing library for REST based services or HTTP handlers that supports mocking external http calls and rendering of sequence diagrams.
- [arch-go](https://github.com/arch-go/arch-go) ⭐ 267 - Updated Feb 2026: Architecture testing tool for Go projects.
- [assert](https://github.com/go-playground/assert) ⭐ 68 - Updated Sep 2022: Basic Assertion Library used along side native go testing, with building blocks for custom assertions.
- [baloo](https://github.com/h2non/baloo) ⭐ 779 - Updated Aug 2022: Expressive and versatile end-to-end HTTP API testing made easy.
- [be](https://github.com/carlmjohnson/be) ⭐ 133 - Updated Sep 2025: The minimalist generic test assertion library.
- [biff](https://github.com/fulldump/biff) ⭐ 14 - Updated Jan 2023: Bifurcation testing framework, BDD compatible.
- [charlatan](https://github.com/percolate/charlatan) ⭐ 205 - Updated Mar 2023: Tool to generate fake interface implementations for tests.
- [commander](https://github.com/SimonBaeumer/commander) ⭐ 231 - Updated Apr 2024: Tool for testing cli applications on windows, linux and osx.
- [cupaloy](https://github.com/bradleyjkemp/cupaloy) ⭐ 332 - Updated Sep 2022: Simple snapshot testing addon for your test framework.
- [dbcleaner](https://github.com/khaiql/dbcleaner) ⭐ 163 - Updated Nov 2021: Clean database for testing purpose, inspired by database_cleaner in Ruby.
- [dft](https://github.com/abecodes/dft) ⭐ 19 - Updated Jan 2025: Lightweight, zero dependency docker containers for testing (or more).
- [dsunit](https://github.com/viant/dsunit) ⭐ 46 - Updated Dec 2025: Datastore testing for SQL, NoSQL, structured files.
- [embedded-postgres](https://github.com/fergusstrange/embedded-postgres) ⭐ 1209 - Updated Mar 2026: Run a real Postgres database locally on Linux, OSX or Windows as part of another Go application or test.
- [endly](https://github.com/viant/endly) ⭐ 268 - Updated Apr 2026: Declarative end to end functional testing.
- [envite](https://github.com/PerimeterX/envite) ⭐ 5 - Updated Jun 2026: Dev and testing environment management framework.
- [fixenv](https://github.com/rekby/fixenv) ⭐ 34 - Updated Oct 2025: Fixture manage engine, inspired by pytest fixtures.

The clean, easy-to-use API enables developers to programmatically define containers that should be run as part of a test and clean up those resources when the test is done.

## Text Processing
_Libraries for parsing and manipulating texts._
### Formatters

- [address](https://github.com/bojanz/address) ⭐ 83 - Updated Feb 2026: Handles address representation, validation and formatting.
- [align](https://github.com/Guitarbum722/align) ⭐ 84 - Updated Sep 2021: A general purpose application that aligns text.
- [bytes](https://github.com/labstack/gommon/tree/master/bytes): Formats and parses numeric byte values (10K, 2M, 3G, etc.).
- [go-fixedwidth](https://github.com/ianlopshire/go-fixedwidth) ⭐ 88 - Updated Feb 2024: Fixed-width text formatting (encoder/decoder with reflection).
- [go-humanize](https://github.com/dustin/go-humanize) ⭐ 4809 - Updated Nov 2025: Formatters for time, numbers, and memory size to human readable format.
- [gotabulate](https://github.com/bndr/gotabulate) ⭐ 339 - Updated Feb 2021: Easily pretty-print your tabular data with Go.
- [sq](https://github.com/neilotoole/sq) ⭐ 2537 - Updated Jul 2026: Convert data from SQL databases or document formats like CSV or Excel into formats such as JSON, Excel, CSV, HTML, Markdown, XML, and YAML.
- [textwrap](https://github.com/isbm/textwrap) ⭐ 7 - Updated Jul 2019: Wraps text at end of lines. Implementation of textwrap module from Python.
### Markup Languages

- [bafi](https://github.com/mmalcek/bafi) ⭐ 116 - Updated Nov 2025: Universal JSON, BSON, YAML, XML translator to ANY format using templates.
- [bbConvert](https://github.com/CalebQ42/bbConvert) ⭐ 12 - Updated Dec 2024: Converts bbCode to HTML that allows you to add support for custom bbCode tags.
- [blackfriday](https://github.com/russross/blackfriday) ⭐ 5611 - Updated Oct 2020: Markdown processor in Go.
- [go-output-format](https://github.com/drewstinnett/go-output-format) ⭐ 18 - Updated Feb 2024: Output go structures into multiple formats (YAML/JSON/etc) in your command line app.
- [go-toml](https://github.com/pelletier/go-toml) ⭐ 1963 - Updated Jul 2026: Go library for the TOML format with query support and handy cli tools.
- [goldmark](https://github.com/yuin/goldmark) ⭐ 4906 - Updated Jul 2026: A Markdown parser written in Go. Easy to extend, standard (CommonMark) compliant, well structured.
- [goq](https://github.com/andrewstuart/goq) ⭐ 270 - Updated Sep 2021: Declarative unmarshalling of HTML using struct tags with jQuery syntax (uses GoQuery).
- [html-to-markdown](https://github.com/JohannesKaufmann/html-to-markdown) ⭐ 3740 - Updated Jun 2026: Convert HTML to Markdown. Even works with entire websites and can be extended through rules.
- [htmlquery](https://github.com/antchfx/htmlquery) ⭐ 784 - Updated May 2026: An XPath query package for HTML, lets you extract data or evaluate from HTML documents by an XPath expression.
- [htmlyaml](https://github.com/nikolaydubina/htmlyaml) ⭐ 6 - Updated Jun 2026: Rich rendering of YAML as HTML in Go.
- [htree](https://github.com/bobg/htree) ⭐ 5 - Updated Dec 2025: Traverse, navigate, filter, and otherwise process trees of html.Node objects.
- [mdsmith](https://github.com/jeduden/mdsmith) ⭐ 10 - Updated Jul 2026: fast, auto-fixing Markdown linter and formatter. Checks style, readability, structure, and cross-file integrity.
- [mxj](https://github.com/clbanning/mxj) ⭐ 629 - Updated Aug 2025: Encode / decode XML as JSON or map[string]interface{}; extract values with dot-notation paths and wildcards. Replaces x2j and j2x packages.
- [toml](https://github.com/BurntSushi/toml) ⭐ 4984 - Updated Jun 2026: TOML configuration format (encoder/decoder with reflection).
### Parsers/Encoders/Decoders

- [allot](https://github.com/sbstjn/allot) ⭐ 60 - Updated Oct 2016: Placeholder and wildcard text parsing for CLI tools and bots.
- [codetree](https://github.com/aerogo/codetree) ⭐ 25 - Updated Oct 2019: Parses indented code (python, pixy, scarlet, etc.) and returns a tree structure.
- [commonregex](https://github.com/mingrammer/commonregex) ⭐ 898 - Updated Nov 2019: A collection of common regular expressions for Go.
- [did](https://github.com/ockam-network/did) ⭐ 95 - Updated Jan 2021: DID (Decentralized Identifiers) Parser and Stringer in Go.
- [doi](https://github.com/hscells/doi) ⭐ 11 - Updated Aug 2017: Document object identifier (doi) parser in Go.
- [editorconfig-core-go](https://github.com/editorconfig/editorconfig-core-go) ⭐ 155 - Updated Jul 2026: Editorconfig file parser and manipulator for Go.
- [encdec](https://github.com/mickep76/encdec): Package provides a generic interface to encoders and decoders.
- [go-fasttld](https://github.com/elliotwutingfeng/go-fasttld) ⭐ 39 - Updated Jul 2026: High performance effective top level domains (eTLD) extraction module.
- [go-nmea](https://github.com/adrianmo/go-nmea) ⭐ 264 - Updated Jun 2026: NMEA parser library for the Go language.
- [go-querystring](https://github.com/google/go-querystring) ⭐ 2144 - Updated Jul 2026: Go library for encoding structs into URL query parameters.
- [go-vcard](https://github.com/emersion/go-vcard) ⭐ 128 - Updated Jun 2026: Parse and format vCard.
- [godump](https://github.com/yassinebenaid/godump) ⭐ 223 - Updated May 2025: Pretty print any GO variable with ease, an alternative to Go's fmt.Printf("%#v").
- [godump (goforj)](https://github.com/goforj/godump) ⭐ 1747 - Updated Jul 2026: Pretty-print Go structs with Laravel/Symfony-style dumps, full type info, colorized CLI output, cycle detection, and private field access.
- [gofeed](https://github.com/mmcdole/gofeed) ⭐ 2850 - Updated Jul 2026: Parse RSS and Atom feeds in Go.
- [gographviz](https://github.com/awalterschulze/gographviz) ⭐ 567 - Updated Feb 2023: Parses the Graphviz DOT language.
- [gonameparts](https://github.com/polera/gonameparts) ⭐ 43 - Updated Sep 2024: Parses human names into individual name parts.
- [ltsv](https://github.com/Wing924/ltsv) ⭐ 9 - Updated Sep 2024: High performance LTSV (Labeled Tab Separated Value) reader for Go.
- [normalize](https://github.com/avito-tech/normalize) ⭐ 53 - Updated Mar 2021: Sanitize, normalize and compare fuzzy text.
- [parseargs-go](https://github.com/nproc/parseargs-go) ⭐ 10 - Updated Jan 2017: string argument parser that understands quotes and backslashes.
- [prattle](https://github.com/askeladdk/prattle) ⭐ 9 - Updated Oct 2025: Scan and parse LL(1) grammars simply and efficiently.
- [sh](https://github.com/mvdan/sh) ⭐ 8907 - Updated Jul 2026: Shell parser and formatter.
- [tokenizer](https://github.com/bzick/tokenizer) ⭐ 141 - Updated Jul 2026: Parse any string, slice or infinite buffer to any tokens.
- [vdf](https://github.com/andygrunwald/vdf) ⭐ 66 - Updated Jun 2026: A Lexer and Parser for Valves Data Format (known as vdf) written in Go.
- [when](https://github.com/olebedev/when) ⭐ 1463 - Updated Mar 2025: Natural EN and RU language date/time parser with pluggable rules.
- [xj2go](https://github.com/stackerzzq/xj2go) ⭐ 36 - Updated Oct 2021: Convert xml or json to go struct.
### Regular Expressions

- [coregex](https://github.com/coregx/coregex) ⭐ 242 - Updated Jun 2026: Production regex engine with Rust regex-crate architecture: multi-engine DFA/NFA, SIMD prefilters, drop-in stdlib replacement.
- [genex](https://github.com/alixaxel/genex) ⭐ 77 - Updated Jan 2020: Count and expand Regular Expressions into all matching Strings.
- [go-wildcard](https://github.com/IGLOU-EU/go-wildcard) ⭐ 103 - Updated May 2026: Simple and lightweight wildcard pattern matching.
- [goregen](https://github.com/zach-klippenstein/goregen) ⭐ 92 - Updated Mar 2016: Library for generating random strings from regular expressions.
- [regroup](https://github.com/oriser/regroup) ⭐ 150 - Updated Sep 2024: Match regex expression named groups into go struct using struct tags and automatic parsing.
- [rex](https://github.com/hedhyw/rex) ⭐ 214 - Updated Dec 2025: Regular expressions builder.
### Sanitation

- [bluemonday](https://github.com/microcosm-cc/bluemonday) ⭐ 3697 - Updated Apr 2025: HTML Sanitizer.

### Scrapers

- [go-sitemap-parser](https://github.com/aafeher/go-sitemap-parser) ⭐ 7 - Updated Jul 2026: Go language library for parsing Sitemaps.
- [GoQuery](https://github.com/PuerkitoBio/goquery) ⭐ 14976 - Updated Jul 2026: GoQuery brings a syntax and a set of features similar to jQuery to the Go language.
- [pagser](https://github.com/foolin/pagser) ⭐ 111 - Updated Oct 2023: Pagser is a simple, extensible, configurable parse and deserialize html page to struct based on goquery and struct tags for golang crawler.
- [Tagify](https://github.com/zoomio/tagify) ⭐ 39 - Updated Jul 2024: Produces a set of tags from given source.
- [walker](https://github.com/cyucelen/walker) ⭐ 14 - Updated Feb 2023: Seamlessly fetch paginated data from any source. Simple and high performance API scraping included.
- [xurls](https://github.com/mvdan/xurls) ⭐ 1267 - Updated Mar 2026: Extract urls from text.
### RSS

- [podcast](https://github.com/eduncan911/podcast) ⭐ 140 - Updated Nov 2020: iTunes Compliant and RSS 2.0 Podcast Generator in Golang
### Utility/Miscellaneous

- [ahocorasick](https://github.com/coregx/ahocorasick) ⭐ 25 - Updated Mar 2026: High-performance Aho-Corasick multi-pattern string matching with DFA compilation and SIMD prefilter, up to 7 GB/s throughput (part of coregx ecosystem).
- [go-runewidth](https://github.com/mattn/go-runewidth) ⭐ 713 - Updated May 2026: Functions to get fixed width of the character or string.
- [kace](https://github.com/codemodus/kace) ⭐ 22 - Updated Aug 2018: Common case conversions covering common initialisms.
- [lancet](https://github.com/duke-git/lancet) ⭐ 5299 - Updated Mar 2026: A comprehensive, Lodash-like utility library for Go
- [petrovich](https://github.com/striker2000/petrovich) ⭐ 51 - Updated Nov 2023: Petrovich is the library which inflects Russian names to given grammatical case.
- [radix](https://github.com/yourbasic/radix) ⭐ 197 - Updated Mar 2018: Fast string sorting algorithm.
- [TySug](https://github.com/Dynom/TySug) ⭐ 20 - Updated Feb 2023: Alternative suggestions with respect to keyboard layouts.
- [uniwidth](https://github.com/unilibs/uniwidth) ⭐ 8 - Updated Mar 2026: High-performance Unicode character width calculation with SWAR optimization, O(1) lookup tables, and ZWJ emoji support.
- [w2vgrep](https://github.com/arunsupe/semantic-grep) ⭐ 1241 - Updated Aug 2024: A semantic grep tool using word embeddings to find semantically similar matches. For example, searching for "death" will find "dead", "killing", "murder".

## Third-party APIs
_Libraries for accessing third party APIs._

- [airtable](https://github.com/mehanizm/airtable) ⭐ 86 - Updated Mar 2025: Go client library for the Airtable API.

- [aws-encryption-sdk-go](https://github.com/chainifynet/aws-encryption-sdk-go) ⭐ 23 - Updated Jun 2025: Unofficial Go SDK implementation of the AWS Encryption SDK.
- [aws-sdk-go](https://github.com/aws/aws-sdk-go-v2) ⭐ 3610 - Updated Jul 2026: The official AWS SDK for the Go programming language.
- [bqwriter](https://github.com/OTA-Insight/bqwriter) ⭐ 16 - Updated Sep 2023: High Level Go Library to write data into Google BigQuery at a high throughout.
- [brewerydb](https://github.com/naegelejd/brewerydb) ⭐ 20 - Updated Jun 2015: Go library for accessing the BreweryDB API.
- [cachet](https://github.com/andygrunwald/cachet) ⭐ 90 - Updated Jun 2021: Go client library for Cachet (open source status page system).
- [circleci](https://github.com/jszwedko/go-circleci) ⭐ 65 - Updated Jan 2024: Go client library for interacting with CircleCI's API.
- [clarifai](https://github.com/samuelcouch/clarifai): Go client library for interfacing with the Clarifai API.
- [codeship-go](https://github.com/codeship/codeship-go) ⭐ 18 - Updated Nov 2020: Go client library for interacting with Codeship's API v2.

## UUID
_Libraries for working with UUIDs._

- [fastuuid](https://github.com/rekby/fastuuid) ⭐ 1 - Updated Feb 2023: Fast generate UUIDv4 as string or bytes.
- [goid](https://github.com/jakehl/goid) ⭐ 41 - Updated Feb 2019: Generate and Parse RFC4122 compliant V4 UUIDs.
- [gouid](https://github.com/twharmon/gouid) ⭐ 27 - Updated Feb 2026: Generate cryptographically secure random string IDs with just one allocation.
- [guid](https://github.com/sdrapkin/guid) ⭐ 75 - Updated Jul 2026: Fast cryptographically safe Guid generator for Go (~10x faster than uuid).
- [nanoid](https://github.com/aidarkhanov/nanoid) ⭐ 62 - Updated Sep 2021 - ⚠️ Archived: A tiny and efficient Go unique string ID generator.
- [sno](https://github.com/muyo/sno) ⭐ 94 - Updated Nov 2021: Compact, sortable and fast unique IDs with embedded metadata.
- [ulid](https://github.com/oklog/ulid) ⭐ 5046 - Updated Apr 2024: Go implementation of ULID (Universally Unique Lexicographically Sortable Identifier).
- [uniq](https://gitlab.com/skilstak/code/go/uniq): No hassle safe, fast unique identifiers with commands.
- [uuid](https://github.com/agext/uuid) ⭐ 18 - Updated Mar 2020: Generate, encode, and decode UUIDs v1 with fast or cryptographic-quality random node identifier.
- [uuid](https://github.com/gofrs/uuid) ⭐ 1814 - Updated Mar 2026: Implementation of Universally Unique Identifier (UUID). Supports both creation and parsing of UUIDs. Actively maintained fork of satori uuid.
- [uuid](https://github.com/google/uuid) ⭐ 6118 - Updated Nov 2024: Go package for UUIDs based on RFC 4122 and DCE 1.1: Authentication and Security Services.
- [uuidcheck](https://github.com/ashwingopalsamy/uuidcheck) ⭐ 6 - Updated Dec 2024: A tiny, dependency-free Go library that validates UUIDs against standard RFC 4122 formatting, converts UUIDv7() into UTC timestamps.
- [wuid](https://github.com/edwingeng/wuid) ⭐ 545 - Updated Jan 2024: An extremely fast globally unique number generator.
- [xid](https://github.com/rs/xid) ⭐ 4280 - Updated Mar 2026: Xid is a globally unique id generator library, ready to be safely used directly in your server code.

## Validation
_Libraries for validation._

- [checkdigit](https://github.com/osamingo/checkdigit) ⭐ 114 - Updated Mar 2025: Provide check digit algorithms (Luhn, Verhoeff, Damm) and calculators (ISBN, EAN, JAN, UPC, etc.).
- [go-validator](https://github.com/tiendc/go-validator) ⭐ 31 - Updated Nov 2024: Validation library using Generics.
- [gody](https://github.com/guiferpa/gody) ⭐ 181 - Updated May 2025: :balloon: A lightweight struct validator for Go.
- [govalid](https://github.com/twharmon/govalid) ⭐ 119 - Updated Jun 2026: Fast, tag-based validation for structs.
- [govalidator](https://github.com/asaskevich/govalidator) ⭐ 6210 - Updated Apr 2026: Validators and sanitizers for strings, numerics, slices and structs.
- [govalidator](https://github.com/thedevsaddam/govalidator) ⭐ 1344 - Updated Apr 2020: Validate Golang request data with simple rules. Highly inspired by Laravel's request validation.
- [govy](https://github.com/nobl9/govy) ⭐ 52 - Updated Jul 2026: strongly-typed validation rules over functional interface, powered by generics and reflection free with heavy focus on crafting clear and information-rich error messages.
- [jio](https://github.com/faceair/jio) ⭐ 126 - Updated Jul 2024: jio is a json schema validator similar to joi.
- [ozzo-validation](https://github.com/go-ozzo/ozzo-validation) ⭐ 4111 - Updated Oct 2020: Supports validation of various data types (structs, strings, maps, slices, etc.) with configurable and extensible validation rules specified in usual code constructs instead of struct tags.
- [validate](https://github.com/gookit/validate) ⭐ 1160 - Updated Jun 2026: Go package for data validation and filtering. support validate Map, Struct, Request(Form, JSON, url.Values, Uploaded Files) data and more features.
- [validate](https://github.com/gobuffalo/validate) ⭐ 94 - Updated Sep 2022: This package provides a framework for writing validations for Go applications.
- [validator](https://github.com/go-playground/validator) ⭐ 20077 - Updated Jul 2026: Go Struct and Field validation, including Cross Field, Cross Struct, Map, Slice and Array diving.
- [Validator](https://github.com/go-the-way/validator) ⭐ 7 - Updated Aug 2024: A lightweight model validator written in Go.Contains VFs:Min, Max, MinLength, MaxLength, Length, Enum, Regex.
- [Zog](https://github.com/Oudwins/zog) ⭐ 1200 - Updated Jul 2026: A Zod inspired schema builder for runtime value parsing and validation.

## Web Frameworks
_Full stack web frameworks._

- [Atreugo](https://github.com/savsgio/atreugo) ⭐ 1304 - Updated Jan 2025: High performance and extensible micro web framework with zero memory allocations in hot paths.
- [Barf](https://github.com/opensaucerer/barf) ⭐ 105 - Updated Dec 2023: Basically, A Remarkable Framework for building JSON-based web APIs. It is entirely unobtrusive and re-invents no wheel. It is crafted such that getting started is easy and quick while being flexible enough for more complex use cases.
- [Beego](https://github.com/beego/beego) ⭐ 32414 - Updated Mar 2026: beego is an open-source, high-performance web framework for the Go programming language.
- [Confetti Framework](https://confetti-framework.github.io/docs/): Confetti is a Go web application framework with an expressive, elegant syntax. Confetti combines the elegance of Laravel and the simplicity of Go.
- [Don](https://github.com/abemedia/go-don) ⭐ 60 - Updated Jul 2026: A highly performant and simple to use API framework.
- [doors](https://github.com/doors-dev/doors) ⭐ 114 - Updated Jul 2026: Server-driven framework for building stateful, reactive web applications entirely in Go.
- [Echo](https://github.com/labstack/echo) ⭐ 32530 - Updated Jul 2026: High performance, minimalist Go web framework.
- [Fastschema](https://github.com/fastschema/fastschema) ⭐ 563 - Updated Jun 2026: A flexible Go web framework and Headless CMS.
- [Fiber](https://github.com/gofiber/fiber) ⭐ 39974 - Updated Jul 2026: An Express.js inspired web framework build on Fasthttp.
- [Flamingo](https://github.com/i-love-flamingo/flamingo) ⭐ 559 - Updated Jul 2026: Framework for pluggable web projects. Including a concept for modules and offering features for DI, Configareas, i18n, template engines, graphql, observability, security, events, routing & reverse routing etc.
- [Flamingo Commerce](https://github.com/i-love-flamingo/flamingo-commerce) ⭐ 590 - Updated Jul 2026: Providing e-commerce features using clean architecture like DDD and ports and adapters, that you can use to build flexible e-commerce applications.
- [Fuego](https://github.com/go-fuego/fuego) ⭐ 1753 - Updated Jun 2026: The framework for busy Go developers! Web framework generating OpenAPI 3 spec from source code.

### Middlewares

- [client-timing](https://github.com/posener/client-timing) ⭐ 25 - Updated Feb 2018: An HTTP client for Server-Timing header.
- [CORS](https://github.com/rs/cors) ⭐ 2895 - Updated Jun 2026: Easily add CORS capabilities to your API.
- [echo-middleware](https://github.com/faabiosr/echo-middleware) ⭐ 16 - Updated Sep 2024: Middleware for Echo framework with logging and metrics.
- [formjson](https://github.com/rs/formjson) ⭐ 38 - Updated Dec 2015: Transparently handle JSON input as a standard form POST.
- [go-fault](https://github.com/github/go-fault) ⭐ 555 - Updated Jul 2026: Fault injection middleware for Go.
- [Limiter](https://github.com/ulule/limiter) ⭐ 2340 - Updated Oct 2024: Dead simple rate limit middleware for Go.
- [ln-paywall](https://github.com/philippgille/ln-paywall) ⭐ 157 - Updated Oct 2018: Go middleware for monetizing APIs on a per-request basis with the Lightning Network (Bitcoin).
- [mid](https://github.com/bobg/mid) ⭐ 10 - Updated Mar 2025: Miscellaneous HTTP middleware features: idiomatic error return from handlers; receive/respond with JSON data; request tracing; and more.
- [rk-gin](https://github.com/rookie-ninja/rk-gin) ⭐ 51 - Updated Apr 2024: Middleware for Gin framework with logging, metrics, auth, tracing etc.
- [rk-grpc](https://github.com/rookie-ninja/rk-grpc) ⭐ 81 - Updated Oct 2023: Middleware for gRPC with logging, metrics, auth, tracing etc.
- [Tollbooth](https://github.com/didip/tollbooth) ⭐ 2859 - Updated Jan 2025: Rate limit HTTP request handler.
- [XFF](https://github.com/sebest/xff) ⭐ 100 - Updated Jan 2021: Handle X-Forwarded-For header and friends.
- [alice](https://github.com/justinas/alice) ⭐ 3361 - Updated Apr 2024: Painless middleware chaining for Go.
- [catena](https://github.com/codemodus/catena) ⭐ 9 - Updated Aug 2018: http.Handler wrapper catenation (same API as "chain").
- [chain](https://github.com/codemodus/chain) ⭐ 61 - Updated Aug 2018: Handler wrapper chaining with scoped data (net/context-based "middleware").
- [gores](https://github.com/alioygur/gores) ⭐ 106 - Updated Jan 2021: Go package that handles HTML, JSON, XML and etc. responses. Useful for RESTful APIs.
- [interpose](https://github.com/carbocation/interpose) ⭐ 291 - Updated Dec 2016: Minimalist net/http middleware for golang.
- [mediary](https://github.com/HereMobilityDevelopers/mediary) ⭐ 88 - Updated Jun 2020: add interceptors to http.Client to allow dumping/shaping/tracing/... of requests/responses.
- [muxchain](https://github.com/stephens2424/muxchain) ⭐ 206 - Updated Feb 2019: Lightweight middleware for net/http.
- [negroni](https://github.com/urfave/negroni) ⭐ 7529 - Updated May 2025: Idiomatic HTTP middleware for Golang.
- [render](https://github.com/unrolled/render) ⭐ 1998 - Updated May 2026: Go package for easily rendering JSON, XML, and HTML template responses.
- [renderer](https://github.com/thedevsaddam/renderer) ⭐ 261 - Updated Apr 2026: Simple, lightweight and faster response (JSON, JSONP, XML, YAML, HTML, File) rendering package for Go.
- [stats](https://github.com/thoas/stats) ⭐ 594 - Updated Apr 2019: Go middleware that stores various information about your web application.
### Routers

- [alien](https://github.com/gernest/alien) ⭐ 134 - Updated Mar 2024: Lightweight and fast http router from outer space.
- [bellt](https://github.com/GuilhermeCaruso/bellt) ⭐ 55 - Updated Jul 2022: A simple Go HTTP router.
- [Bone](https://github.com/go-zoo/bone) ⭐ 1284 - Updated Apr 2019: Lightning Fast HTTP Multiplexer.
- [Bxog](https://github.com/claygod/Bxog) ⭐ 104 - Updated Jun 2026: Simple and fast HTTP router for Go. It works with routes of varying difficulty, length and nesting. And he knows how to create a URL from the received parameters.
- [chi](https://github.com/go-chi/chi) ⭐ 22548 - Updated Jul 2026: Small, fast and expressive HTTP router built on net/context.
- [fasthttprouter](https://github.com/buaazp/fasthttprouter) ⭐ 869 - Updated Jan 2019: High performance router forked from httprouter. The first router fit for fasthttp.
- [FastRouter](https://github.com/razonyang/fastrouter) ⭐ 25 - Updated Nov 2017: a fast, flexible HTTP router written in Go.
- [Fox](https://github.com/fox-toolkit/fox) ⭐ 14 - Updated Jul 2026: A high-performance HTTP router for building reverse proxies and API gateways, with first-class support for mutating routes at runtime.
- [fursy](https://github.com/coregx/fursy) ⭐ 7 - Updated Jul 2026: HTTP router with type-safe generic handlers, automatic OpenAPI 3.1 generation from code, and RFC 9457 error responses.
- [goblin](https://github.com/bmf-san/goblin) ⭐ 82 - Updated Dec 2024: A golang http router based on trie tree.
- [gocraft/web](https://github.com/gocraft/web) ⭐ 1523 - Updated Feb 2019: Mux and middleware package in Go.
- [Goji](https://github.com/goji/goji) ⭐ 974 - Updated Jan 2019: Goji is a minimalistic and flexible HTTP request multiplexer with support for net/context.
- [GoLobby/Router](https://github.com/golobby/router) ⭐ 22 - Updated Mar 2022: GoLobby Router is a lightweight yet powerful HTTP router for the Go programming language.
- [goroute](https://github.com/goroute/route) ⭐ 9 - Updated Dec 2019: Simple yet powerful HTTP request multiplexer.
- [GoRouter](https://github.com/vardius/gorouter) ⭐ 153 - Updated Sep 2024: GoRouter is a Server/API micro framework, HTTP request router, multiplexer, mux that provides request router with middleware supporting net/context.
- [gowww/router](https://github.com/gowww/router) ⭐ 185 - Updated Sep 2023: Lightning fast HTTP router fully compatible with the net/http.Handler interface.
- [httprouter](https://github.com/julienschmidt/httprouter) ⭐ 17136 - Updated Jan 2024: High performance router. Use this and the standard http handlers to form a very high performance web framework.
- [httptreemux](https://github.com/dimfeld/httptreemux) ⭐ 618 - Updated Jul 2024: High-speed, flexible tree-based HTTP router for Go. Inspiration from httprouter.
- [lars](https://github.com/go-playground/lars) ⭐ 385 - Updated Oct 2017: Is a lightweight, fast and extensible zero allocation HTTP router for Go used to create customizable frameworks.
- [mux](https://github.com/gorilla/mux) ⭐ 21842 - Updated Jun 2024: Powerful URL router and dispatcher for golang.
- [nchi](https://github.com/muir/nchi) ⭐ 19 - Updated Apr 2026: chi-like router built on httprouter with dependency injection based middleware wrappers
- [ngamux](https://github.com/ngamux/ngamux) ⭐ 71 - Updated Feb 2026: Simple HTTP router for Go.
- [ozzo-routing](https://github.com/go-ozzo/ozzo-routing) ⭐ 452 - Updated Sep 2021: An extremely fast Go (golang) HTTP router that supports regular expression route matching. Comes with full support for building RESTful APIs.
- [pure](https://github.com/go-playground/pure) ⭐ 153 - Updated Jul 2023: Is a lightweight HTTP router that sticks to the std "net/http" implementation.
- [Siesta](https://github.com/VividCortex/siesta) ⭐ 347 - Updated Apr 2021: Composable framework to write middleware and handlers.
- [vestigo](https://github.com/husobee/vestigo) ⭐ 265 - Updated Oct 2020: Performant, stand-alone, HTTP compliant URL Router for go web applications.
- [violetear](https://github.com/nbari/violetear) ⭐ 107 - Updated Sep 2022 - ⚠️ Archived: Go HTTP router.
- [xmux](https://github.com/rs/xmux) ⭐ 100 - Updated Jun 2017: High performance muxer based on httprouter with net/context support.
- [xujiajun/gorouter](https://github.com/xujiajun/gorouter) ⭐ 525 - Updated Sep 2019: A simple and fast HTTP router for Go.

## Zero Trust
_Libraries and tools to implement Zero Trust architectures._

- [Cosign](https://github.com/sigstore/cosign) ⭐ 6141 - Updated Jul 2026: Container Signing, Verification and Storage in an OCI registry.

- [OpenZiti](https://github.com/openziti/ziti) ⭐ 4296 - Updated Jul 2026: A full, open source zero trust overlay network. Including numerous SDKs for numerous languages such as golang allowing you to embed zero trust principles directly into your applications. The OpenZiti Test Kitchen has numerous examples to draw inspiration from including a zero trust ssh client - zssh
- [Spiffe-Vault](https://github.com/philips-labs/spiffe-vault) ⭐ 101 - Updated Jul 2026: Utilizes Spiffe JWT authentication with Hashicorp Vault for secretless authentication.
- [Spire](https://github.com/spiffe/spire) ⭐ 2439 - Updated Jul 2026: SPIRE (the SPIFFE Runtime Environment) is a toolchain of APIs for establishing trust between software systems across a wide variety of hosting platforms.

## Code Analysis
_Source code analysis tools, also known as Static Application Security Testing (SAST) Tools._

- [apicompat](https://github.com/bradleyfalzon/apicompat) ⭐ 182 - Updated Feb 2017: Checks recent changes to a Go project for backwards incompatible changes.
- [asty](https://github.com/asty-org/asty) ⭐ 88 - Updated May 2023: Converts golang AST to JSON and JSON to AST.
- [blanket](https://gitlab.com/verygoodsoftwarenotvirus/blanket) ⭐ 2 - Updated Jul 2021: blanket is a tool that helps you catch functions which don't have direct unit tests in your Go packages.
- [ChainJacking](https://github.com/Checkmarx/chainjacking) ⭐ 64 - Updated May 2026: Find which of your Go lang direct GitHub dependencies is susceptible to ChainJacking attack.
- [Chronos](https://github.com/amit-davidson/Chronos) ⭐ 441 - Updated Apr 2022: Detects race conditions statically
- [dupl](https://github.com/mibk/dupl) ⭐ 368 - Updated Mar 2026: Tool for code clone detection.
- [errcheck](https://github.com/kisielk/errcheck) ⭐ 2525 - Updated May 2026: Errcheck is a program for checking for unchecked errors in Go programs.
- [fatcontext](https://github.com/Crocmagnon/fatcontext) ⭐ 80 - Updated Jun 2026: Fatcontext detects nested contexts in loops or function literals.
- [go-checkstyle](https://github.com/qiniu/checkstyle) ⭐ 130 - Updated Nov 2018: checkstyle is a style check tool like java checkstyle. This tool inspired by java checkstyle, golint. The style referred to some points in Go Code Review Comments.
- [go-cleanarch](https://github.com/roblaszczak/go-cleanarch) ⭐ 983 - Updated Nov 2021: go-cleanarch was created to validate Clean Architecture rules, like a The Dependency Rule and interaction between packages in your Go projects.
- [go-critic](https://github.com/go-critic/go-critic) ⭐ 2058 - Updated Jun 2026: source code linter that brings checks that are currently not implemented in other linters.
- [go-mod-outdated](https://github.com/psampaz/go-mod-outdated) ⭐ 671 - Updated Feb 2023: An easy way to find outdated dependencies of your Go projects.
- [goast-viewer](https://github.com/yuroyoro/goast-viewer) ⭐ 793 - Updated May 2019: Web based Golang AST visualizer.
- [goimports](https://pkg.go.dev/golang.org/x/tools/cmd/goimports): Tool to fix (add, remove) your Go imports automatically.
- [golang-ifood-sdk](https://github.com/arxdsilva/golang-ifood-sdk) ⭐ 13 - Updated Apr 2022: iFood API SDK.
- [golangci-lint](https://github.com/golangci/golangci-lint) ⭐ 19189 - Updated Jul 2026: A fast Go linters runner. It runs linters in parallel, uses caching, supports yaml config, has integrations with all major IDE and has dozens of linters included.
- [golines](https://github.com/segmentio/golines) ⭐ 1133 - Updated Dec 2025 - ⚠️ Archived: Formatter that automatically shortens long lines in Go code.
- [gomarklint](https://github.com/shinagawa-web/gomarklint) ⭐ 19 - Updated Jul 2026: Markdown linter with built-in HTTP link validation, single binary, no Node.js required.
- [GoPlantUML](https://github.com/jfeliu007/goplantuml) ⭐ 2093 - Updated Sep 2025: Library and CLI that generates text plantump class diagram containing information about structures and interfaces with the relationship among them.
- [goreturns](https://github.com/sqs/goreturns) ⭐ 538 - Updated Oct 2023: Adds zero-value return statements to match the func return types.
- [gostatus](https://github.com/shurcooL/gostatus) ⭐ 245 - Updated May 2025: Command line tool, shows the status of repositories that contain Go packages.
- [lint](https://github.com/surullabs/lint) ⭐ 66 - Updated Oct 2017: Run linters as part of go test.
- [php-parser](https://github.com/z7zmey/php-parser) ⭐ 959 - Updated Feb 2021: A Parser for PHP written in Go.
- [revive](https://github.com/mgechev/revive) ⭐ 5536 - Updated Jul 2026: ~6x faster, stricter, configurable, extensible, and beautiful drop-in replacement for golint.
- [staticcheck](https://github.com/dominikh/go-tools/tree/master/cmd/staticcheck): staticcheck is go vet on steroids, applying a ton of static analysis checks you might be used to from tools like ReSharper for C#.
- [structalign](https://github.com/peczenyj/structalign) ⭐ 9 - Updated Jun 2026: Shows how a struct's fields could be reordered to use less memory, printing a diff instead of rewriting files.
- [stto](https://github.com/mainak55512/stto) ⭐ 47 - Updated Nov 2025: A light-weight superfast line of code counter written in pure Go.
- [testifylint](https://github.com/Antonboom/testifylint) ⭐ 173 - Updated Jul 2026: A linter that checks usage of github.com/stretchr/testify.
- [tickgit](https://github.com/augmentable-dev/tickgit) ⭐ 324 - Updated Jun 2020: CLI and go package for surfacing code comment TODOs (in any language) and applying a git blameto identify the author.
- [todocheck](https://github.com/preslavmihaylov/todocheck) ⭐ 439 - Updated Jun 2026: Static code analyser which links TODO comments in code with issues in your issue tracker.
- [unconvert](https://github.com/mdempsky/unconvert) ⭐ 388 - Updated Feb 2025: Remove unnecessary type conversions from Go source.
- [usestdlibvars](https://github.com/sashamelentyev/usestdlibvars) ⭐ 48 - Updated May 2025: A linter that detect the possibility to use variables/constants from the Go standard library.
- [vacuum](https://github.com/daveshanley/vacuum) ⭐ 1101 - Updated Jul 2026: An ultra-super-fast, lightweight OpenAPI linter and quality checking tool.
- [validate](https://github.com/mccoyst/validate) ⭐ 62 - Updated Aug 2023: Automatically validates struct fields with tags.
- [wrapcheck](https://github.com/tomarrell/wrapcheck) ⭐ 375 - Updated Nov 2025: A linter to check that errors from external packages are wrapped.

- [GoDocTooltip](https://github.com/diankong/GoDocTooltip) ⭐ 13 - Updated Dec 2022: Chrome extension for Go Doc sites, which shows function description as tooltip at function list.
- [Gokapi](https://github.com/Forceu/gokapi) ⭐ 2802 - Updated Jul 2026: Lightweight server to share files, which expire after a set amount of downloads or days. Similar to Firefox Send, but without public upload.
- [GoLand](https://jetbrains.com/go): Full featured cross-platform Go IDE.
- [GoNB](https://github.com/janpfeifer/gonb) ⭐ 1031 - Updated Jun 2026: Interactive Go programming with Jupyter Notebooks (also works in VSCode, Binder and Google's Colab).
- [GooseForum](https://github.com/leancodebox/GooseForum) ⭐ 114 - Updated Jul 2026: Self-hosted forum platform built with Go, Vue, and Tailwind CSS.
- [Gor](https://github.com/buger/gor) ⭐ 19294 - Updated Apr 2025: Http traffic replication tool, for replaying traffic from production to stage/dev environments in real-time.
- [Guora](https://github.com/meloalright/guora) ⭐ 672 - Updated Jan 2023: A self-hosted Quora like web application written in Go.
- [hoofli](https://github.com/dnnrly/hoofli) ⭐ 11 - Updated Aug 2024: Generate PlantUML diagrams from Chrome or Firefox network inspections.
- [hotswap](https://github.com/edwingeng/hotswap) ⭐ 426 - Updated May 2024: A complete solution to reload your go code without restarting your server, interrupting or blocking any ongoing procedure.
- [hugo](https://gohugo.io/): Fast and Modern Static Website Engine.
- [ide](https://github.com/thestrukture/ide) ⭐ 366 - Updated Nov 2022: Browser accessible IDE. Designed for Go with Go.
- [joincap](https://github.com/assafmo/joincap) ⭐ 220 - Updated Jun 2025: Command-line utility for merging multiple pcap files together.
- [JuiceFS](https://github.com/juicedata/juicefs) ⭐ 14206 - Updated Jul 2026: Distributed POSIX file system built on top of Redis and AWS S3.
- [Juju](https://jujucharms.com/): Cloud-agnostic service deployment and orchestration - supports EC2, Azure, Openstack, MAAS and more.
- [Layli](https://layli.app): Draw pretty layout diagrams as code.
- [Leaps](https://github.com/jeffail/leaps) ⭐ 756 - Updated Feb 2021: Pair programming service using Operational Transforms.
- [lgo](https://github.com/yunabe/lgo) ⭐ 2453 - Updated Jul 2019: Interactive Go programming with Jupyter. It supports code completion, code inspection and 100% Go compatibility.
- [limetext](https://limetext.github.io): Lime Text is a powerful and elegant text editor primarily developed in Go that aims to be a Free and open-source software successor to Sublime Text.
- [LiteIDE](https://github.com/visualfc/liteide) ⭐ 7761 - Updated May 2026: LiteIDE is a simple, open source, cross-platform Go IDE.
- [mac-cleanup-go](https://github.com/2ykwang/mac-cleanup-go) ⭐ 435 - Updated Jul 2026: Preview-first TUI for cleaning macOS caches, logs, and temporary files.
- [mdv](https://github.com/Allra-Fintech/mdv) ⭐ 2 - Updated Jul 2026: CLI tool that renders Markdown files in the browser with live reload, GFM, syntax highlighting, Mermaid diagrams, and PDF export.
- [mockingjay](https://github.com/quii/mockingjay-server) ⭐ 568 - Updated Jan 2021: Fake HTTP servers and consumer driven contracts from one configuration file. You can also make the server randomly misbehave to help do more realistic performance tests.
- [myLG](https://github.com/mehrdadrad/mylg) ⭐ 2718 - Updated Feb 2020: Command Line Network Diagnostic tool written in Go.
- [naclpipe](https://github.com/unix4fun/naclpipe) ⭐ 23 - Updated Nov 2018: Simple NaCL EC25519 based crypto pipe tool written in Go.
- [Neo-cowsay](https://github.com/Code-Hex/Neo-cowsay) ⭐ 342 - Updated Aug 2023: 🐮 cowsay is reborn. for a New Era.
- [nes](https://github.com/fogleman/nes) ⭐ 5652 - Updated Sep 2023: Nintendo Entertainment System (NES) emulator written in Go.
- [onWatch](https://github.com/onllm-dev/onWatch) ⭐ 678 - Updated Jun 2026: Monitor AI API quotas across providers locally with historical tracking, alerts, and a web dashboard to avoid surprise throttling and budget overruns.
- [Orbit](https://github.com/gulien/orbit) ⭐ 187 - Updated Jan 2021: A simple tool for running commands and generating files from templates.
- [peg](https://github.com/pointlander/peg) ⭐ 1112 - Updated May 2026: Peg, Parsing Expression Grammar, is an implementation of a Packrat parser generator.
- [Plik](https://github.com/root-gg/plik) ⭐ 1795 - Updated Jul 2026: Plik is a temporary file upload system (Wetransfer like) in Go.
- [portal](https://github.com/SpatiumPortae/portal) ⭐ 1758 - Updated May 2024: Portal is a quick and easy command-line file transfer utility from any computer to another.
- [restic](https://github.com/restic/restic) ⭐ 35039 - Updated Jul 2026: De-duplicating backup program.
- [sake](https://github.com/alajmo/sake) ⭐ 748 - Updated May 2026: sake is a command runner for local and remote hosts.
- [scc](https://github.com/boyter/scc) ⭐ 8543 - Updated Jul 2026: Sloc Cloc and Code, a very fast accurate code counter with complexity calculations and COCOMO estimates.
- [Seaweed File System](https://github.com/chrislusf/seaweedfs) ⭐ 30 - Updated Feb 2026: Fast, Simple and Scalable Distributed File System with O(1) disk seek.
- [shell2http](https://github.com/msoap/shell2http) ⭐ 1496 - Updated Feb 2026: Executing shell commands via http server (for prototyping or remote control).
- [Snitch](https://github.com/lucasgomide/snitch) ⭐ 16 - Updated Jul 2018: Simple way to notify your team and many tools when someone has deployed any application via Tsuru.
- [sonic](https://github.com/go-sonic/sonic) ⭐ 2112 - Updated Feb 2024: Sonic is a Go Blogging Platform. Simple and Powerful.
- [Stack Up](https://github.com/pressly/sup) ⭐ 2515 - Updated Jan 2022: Stack Up, a super simple deployment tool - just Unix - think of it like 'make' for a network of servers.
- [stew](https://github.com/marwanhawari/stew) ⭐ 352 - Updated May 2025: An independent package manager for compiled binaries.
- [syncthing](https://syncthing.net/): Open, decentralized file synchronization tool and protocol.
- [tcpdog](https://github.com/mehrdadrad/tcpdog) ⭐ 261 - Updated Jul 2021: eBPF based TCP observability.
- [tinycare-tui](https://github.com/DMcP89/tinycare-tui) ⭐ 21 - Updated Mar 2026: Small terminal app that shows git commits from the last 24 hours and week, current weather, some self care advice, a joke, and you current todo list tasks.
- [tldx](https://github.com/brandonyoungdev/tldx) ⭐ 1892 - Updated Jul 2026: Bulk domain availability checker using RDAP, DNS, and WHOIS fallback with keyword permutation generation.
- [toxiproxy](https://github.com/shopify/toxiproxy) ⭐ 12163 - Updated Jul 2026: Proxy to simulate network and system conditions for automated tests.
- [tsuru](https://tsuru.io/): Extensible and open source Platform as a Service software.
- [vaku](https://github.com/lingrino/vaku) ⭐ 160 - Updated Jul 2026: CLI & API for folder-based functions in Vault like copy, move, and search.
- [vFlow](https://github.com/VerizonDigital/vflow) ⭐ 1156 - Updated Aug 2024: High-performance, scalable and reliable IPFIX, sFlow and Netflow collector.
- [Wave Terminal](https://waveterm.dev): Wave is an open-source, AI-native terminal built for seamless developer workflows with inline rendering, a modern UI, and persistent sessions.
- [wellington](https://github.com/wellington/wellington) ⭐ 301 - Updated Sep 2020 - ⚠️ Archived: Sass project management tool, extends the language with sprite functions (like Compass).
- [woke](https://github.com/get-woke/woke) ⭐ 515 - Updated Aug 2022: Detect non-inclusive language in your source code.
- [yai](https://github.com/ekkinox/yai) ⭐ 866 - Updated Dec 2023: AI powered terminal assistant.
- [zs](https://git.mills.io/prologic/zs): an extremely minimal static site generator.

## Benchmarks

- [autobench](https://github.com/davecheney/autobench) ⭐ 100 - Updated Jun 2014: Framework to compare the performance between different Go versions.
- [go-benchmark-app](https://github.com/mrLSD/go-benchmark-app) ⭐ 27 - Updated Mar 2017: Powerful HTTP-benchmark tool mixed with Аb, Wrk, Siege tools. Gathering statistics and various parameters for benchmarks and comparison results.
- [go-benchmarks](https://github.com/tylertreat/go-benchmarks) ⭐ 150 - Updated Feb 2016: Few miscellaneous Go microbenchmarks. Compare some language features to alternative approaches.
- [go-http-routing-benchmark](https://github.com/julienschmidt/go-http-routing-benchmark) ⭐ 1659 - Updated Jul 2020: Go HTTP request router benchmark and comparison.
- [go-json-benchmark](https://github.com/zerosnake0/go-json-benchmark) ⭐ 11 - Updated Oct 2020: Go JSON benchmark.
- [go-ml-benchmarks](https://github.com/nikolaydubina/go-ml-benchmarks) ⭐ 34 - Updated Jun 2026: benchmarks for machine learning inference in Go.
- [go-web-framework-benchmark](https://github.com/smallnest/go-web-framework-benchmark) ⭐ 2138 - Updated Jul 2026: Go web framework benchmark.
- [go_serialization_benchmarks](https://github.com/alecthomas/go_serialization_benchmarks) ⭐ 1627 - Updated Jul 2025: Benchmarks of Go serialization methods.
- [gocostmodel](https://github.com/PuerkitoBio/gocostmodel) ⭐ 63 - Updated May 2021: Benchmarks of common basic operations for the Go language.
- [golang-benchmarks](https://github.com/SimonWaldherr/golang-benchmarks) ⭐ 145 - Updated Jul 2026: a collection of golang benchmarks.
- [golang-sql-benchmark](https://github.com/tyler-smith/golang-sql-benchmark): Collection of benchmarks for popular Go database/SQL utilities.
- [gospeed](https://github.com/feyeleanor/GoSpeed) ⭐ 128 - Updated Mar 2024: Go micro-benchmarks for calculating the speed of language constructs.
- [kvbench](https://github.com/jimrobinson/kvbench) ⭐ 27 - Updated Sep 2019: Key/Value database benchmark.
- [skynet](https://github.com/atemerev/skynet) ⭐ 1062 - Updated Nov 2023: Skynet 1M threads microbenchmark.
- [speedtest-resize](https://github.com/fawick/speedtest-resize) ⭐ 244 - Updated Oct 2020: Compare various Image resize algorithms for the Go language.
- [vizb](https://github.com/goptics/vizb) ⭐ 79 - Updated Jul 2026: A CLI tool to visualize Go benchmark data in 4D.

## E-Books
### E-books for purchase

- [100 Go Mistakes: How to Avoid Them](https://www.manning.com/books/100-go-mistakes-how-to-avoid-them): 
- [Black Hat Go](https://nostarch.com/blackhatgo): Go programming for hackers and pentesters.
- [Build an Orchestrator in Go](https://www.manning.com/books/build-an-orchestrator-in-go): 
- [Continuous Delivery in Go](https://www.manning.com/books/continuous-delivery-in-go): This practical guide to continuous delivery shows you how to rapidly establish an automated pipeline that will improve your testing, code quality, and final product.
- [Creative DIY Microcontroller Project With TinyGo and WebAssembly](https://www.packtpub.com/product/creative-diy-microcontroller-projects-with-tinygo-and-webassembly/9781800560208): An introduction into the TinyGo compiler with projects involving Arduino and WebAssembly.
- [Effective Go: Elegant, efficient, and testable code](https://www.manning.com/books/effective-go): Unlock Go’s unique perspective on program design, and start writing simple, maintainable, and testable Go code.
- [For the Love of Go](https://bitfieldconsulting.com/books/love): An introductory book for Go beginners.
- [Go in Practice, Second Edition](https://www.manning.com/books/go-in-practice-second-edition): Your practical guide on the ins-and-outs of Go development, covering the standard library and the most important tools from Go’s powerful ecosystem.
- [Know Go: Generics](https://bitfieldconsulting.com/books/generics): A guide to understanding and using generics in Go.
- [Lets-Go](https://lets-go.alexedwards.net): A step-by-step guide to creating fast, secure and maintanable web applications with Go.
- [Lets-Go-Further](https://lets-go-further.alexedwards.net): Advanced patterns for building APIs and web applications in Go.
- [The Power of Go: Tests](https://bitfieldconsulting.com/books/tests): A guide to testing in Go.
- [The Power of Go: Tools](https://bitfieldconsulting.com/books/tools): A guide to writing command-line tools in Go.
- [Writing A Compiler In Go](https://compilerbook.com): 
- [Writing An Interpreter In Go](https://interpreterbook.com): Book that introduces dozens of techniques for writing idiomatic, expressive, and efficient Go code that avoids common pitfalls.

### Tutorials

- [50 Shades of Go](https://golang50shades.github.io/): Traps, Gotchas, and Common Mistakes for New Golang Devs.
- [A Comprehensive Guide to Structured Logging in Go](https://betterstack.com/community/guides/logging/logging-in-go/): Delve deep into the world of structured logging in Go with a specific focus on recently accepted slog proposal which aims to bring high performance structured logging with levels to the standard library.
- [A Guide to Golang E-Commerce](https://snipcart.com/blog/golang-ecommerce-ponzu-cms-demo?utm_term=golang-ecommerce-ponzu-cms-demo): Building a Golang site for e-commerce (demo included).

- [Building Go Web Applications and Microservices Using Gin](https://semaphoreci.com/community/tutorials/building-go-web-applications-and-microservices-using-gin): Get familiar with Gin and find out how it can help you reduce boilerplate code and build a request handling pipeline.

### Guided Learning

- [The Go Developer Roadmap](https://roadmap.sh/golang): A visual roadmap that new Go developers can follow through to help them learn Go.
- [The Go Interview Practice](https://github.com/RezaSi/go-interview-practice) ⭐ 2417 - Updated Jul 2026: A GitHub repository offering coding challenges for Go technical interview preparation.
- [The Go Learning Path](https://tutorialedge.net/paths/golang/): A guided learning path containing a mix of free and premium resources.
- [The Go Skill Tree](https://labex.io/skilltrees/go): A structured learning path that combines both free and premium resources.
